<form><strong style="color:darkred; font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size:14pt">瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第六十一</strong></form>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　彌勒菩薩說</span></span></span><br />
<a name="61p4903"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　唐三藏沙門玄奘奉詔譯</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:#000000"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　韓清淨科記</span></span></span><br />
<span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">攝決擇分中有尋有伺等三地之四</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　決擇〈有尋有伺等三地〉，在卷58～60已將此三地中的界建立、及煩惱、業、生三種雜染建立決擇圓滿。現在是決擇〈有尋有伺等三地〉的第四個部分，引用佛陀在經中所說例舉種種譬喻以證成雜染過失及施戒修的功德，又以諸王德失差別、諸苦諦相差別、補特伽羅下中士差別三方面決擇，以導引眾生的身語意三業趣向正行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　決擇諸王德失，出自《出愛王經》，是玄奘大師譯的，在大正藏14冊，不空三藏翻譯的是《佛為優填王說王法政論經》。玄奘大師認為不空三藏譯的優填王是錯誤的，應該譯成「出愛王」。決擇諸苦諦相差別，說明八苦的相狀，是引《八苦經》所說。決擇補特伽羅差別，分兩段，一是三士建立諸門差別，約十一種情況來說明下中上三品人的差別，依《三士經》裡面節錄出來的。另一是十有情眾的愛樂差別，有十種有情眾生，愛樂十種法，是由十有情等各種經文引出來的。卷61等於在讀這三部佛經。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">戊二、引經說3　己一、決擇諸王德失差別2　庚一、出愛王白佛2　辛一、述因緣3　壬一、由觀察2　癸一、於過失</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科引經說，引經所說，分三科；第一科決擇諸王德失差別，決擇諸王的功德過失差別，分二科；第一科出愛王白佛，出，梵語是嗢陀演那；愛，梵語稱為伐蹉，王，梵文稱為褐賴闍，又分二科；第一科述因緣，敘述出愛王向佛說這句話的因緣，分三科；第一科由觀察，由觀察知道德失，又分三科；第一科於過失，於他人呵諫不實過失心不生惱。在大正藏14冊裡面，有很多佛為國王說法的情況，可以從中學到很多智慧。大正藏14冊797頁到799頁有不空三藏譯的這部經，內容很像《出愛王經》，幾乎差不了多少，但是此處少了前文，也少了序，及後面勸說的部分，只引中間那一段。玄奘大師與不空三藏翻譯的有所差異，不是完全一樣，不過大部分是相同的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，如佛世尊為出愛王所說經言：彼王一時往詣佛所，頂禮佛足，白言：世尊！有一沙門、若婆羅門來至我所，以不真實過失，現前呵諫於我，我於爾時，其心不生悔惱憂慼。何以故？觀此過失，於我自身都不見故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如佛世尊為出愛王所說經上說：有一次國王去拜訪佛，到佛那裡向佛頂禮以後，告訴佛陀：世尊！若有一個出家人，或是有學問的婆羅門，來到這裡，以不真實的過失，現前呵斥勸諫於我。我並沒有造作這種過失，對方這樣呵斥、諫誨於我時，我的心並沒有後悔、也沒有懊惱、憂愁、悲慼。為什麼？因為觀察這種過失，在我身上都找不到。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、於功德</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科於功德，於他人所讚不實功德心不生喜。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有沙門、若婆羅門來至我所，以不真實功德，現前讚勸於我，我於爾時，心亦不生歡喜踊躍。何以故？觀此功德，於我自身都不見故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有沙門或婆羅門來到我面前，以不真實的功德，現前讚歎勸勉我說：你很好啊！我在那個時候，心也不會歡喜踊躍。為什麼？因為觀察這種功德，在我身上找不到。修行人也一樣，如果有人忽然來毀謗自己，自己沒有這過失，是不用在意；如果有人忽然來讚歎自己，若是自己沒有功德，也不用高興。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4904"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、由尋伺</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科由尋伺，由籌量尋伺功德過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼諸沙門及婆羅門既退還已，我便獨處空閑靜室，生如是心籌量尋伺：我當云何了知諸王真實過失、真實功德？若我知者，當捨其失，當修其德。誰有沙門、或婆羅門，能了諸王真實過失、真實功德，亦能為我廣開示者？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　那個沙門及婆羅門回去以後，我就自己一個人在空曠寂靜的地方，心裡籌量思惟：我要怎麼樣才能知道諸位國王真實的過失及真實的功德？如果我知道的話，我應該捨掉各種過失，應該修習各種功德。到底有哪一個出家人，或哪一個婆羅門，他能夠真實了解什麼是為王的真實過失及真實功德，也能夠為我廣泛詳細的開示？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬三、由作念</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科由作念，作念向佛請問功德過失之義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">既尋伺已，便作是念：唯我世尊一切知者、一切見者，定當了知諸王所有真實過失、真實功德，我今當往佛世尊所，請問斯義。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　經過籌量思惟後，就這樣想：只有佛陀具足一切種智是一切知者，具足五眼是一切見者，一定通達了知諸王的所有真實過失、真實功德，只有佛陀才能夠開導我這件事情，我應該去佛那裡請問這些道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛二、請問義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科請問義，請問功德過失的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">故我今者來至佛所，請決是義，唯願如來為我開示。世尊！云何諸王真實過失？云何諸王真實功德？作是請已。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　所以我現在來到佛的處所，請問決議其中的道理，希望佛陀為我詳細開示。慈悲偉大的佛！請問什麼是為王的真實過失？什麼是為王的真實功德？這樣請問佛陀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">庚二、佛告出愛王3　辛一、略標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科佛告出愛王，佛開示出愛王德失的道理，分三科；第一科略標，要略標出德失的道理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">爾時，世尊告出愛王曰：大王！大王今者應當了知王之過失、王之功德、王衰損門、王方便門、王可愛法，及能引發王可愛法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　那時，佛陀對出愛王說：大王！大王現在應當了知王的過失、王的功德、王的衰損門、王的方便門、王的可愛法，及如何能夠引發王的可愛法。佛將為他詳細的說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4905"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛二、別釋6　壬一、王之過失2　癸一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別釋，各別的解釋，分六科；第一科王之過失，說明王的過失相，又分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名為王之過失？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為王的過失？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、釋3　子一、標成就</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科標成就，標出國王成就十種過失不可歸仰。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">大王當知！王過失者略有十種。王若成就如是過失，雖有大府庫、有大輔佐、有大軍眾，然不可歸仰。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　大王你應當知道！王的過失要略而言有十種。如果一個國王有這十種過失的話，雖然擁有很多財物、兵甲，國庫充盈的大府庫；有很多賢良大臣的大輔佐；有很多強力勇猛的軍隊，可是不要去歸投依靠仰仗這位國王。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列種類</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列種類，列出十種過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為十？一、種姓不高，二、不得自在，三、立性暴惡，四、猛利憤發，五、恩惠奢薄，六、受邪佞言，七、所作不思不順儀則，八、不顧善法，九、不知差別忘所作恩，十、一向縱任專行放逸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是王的十種過失？一、種姓不高，二、不得自在，三、立性暴惡，四、猛利憤發，五、恩惠奢薄，六、受邪佞言，七、所作不思不順儀則，八、不顧善法，九、不知差別忘所作恩，十、一向縱任專行放逸。這是先列出來十種王的過失，下面各別說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、隨別釋2　丑一、辨相10　寅一、種姓不高</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科隨別釋，各別的解釋，分二科；第一科辨相，說明這十種過失的相貌，又分十科；第一科種姓不高，家族種姓不高貴。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王種姓不高？謂有國王，隨一下類王家而生，非宿尊貴；或雖於此王家而生，賤女之子，不相似子；或是大臣、輔相、國師、群官等子。如是名王種姓不高。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為國王的種姓不高？是指有位國王是隨吠舍、戍陀羅等其中一種低下種類的王家所生，不是高尚的王族所生，非宿尊貴，不是一向以來就很尊貴的傳承；或者他雖然是國王的孩子，然而卻是賤女之子，不是正妃所生。賤女所生之子，與國王不會很相似，如果是正妃所生的真命天子，從小在各方面都受到最好的栽培，形相相似，才稱為相似子；或是大官、宰相、國師、群官等的孩子。這些下類王家等出身的國王，稱作王種姓不高。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4906"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、不得自在</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不得自在，為諸大臣等所制不得自在。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王不得自在？謂有國王，為諸大臣、輔相、國師、群官所制，不隨所欲作所應作，錫賚群臣；於妙五欲，亦不如意歡娛遊戲。如是名王不得自在。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作國王的不得自在？是指有一類國王，被他下面的大臣、輔相、國師、群官所控制，不能隨心所欲作他應該作的事情，不能隨意的賞賜群臣百官。「錫，賚」都是賞賜的意思。於微妙的五欲也不能如意盡情的享受遊戲。這種國王稱為王不得自在。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、立性暴惡2　卯一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科立性暴惡，性情暴惡，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王立性暴惡？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王的個性暴惡？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋3　辰一、辨差別3　巳一、對面暴惡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科辨差別，說明暴惡的差別相，又分三科；第一科對面暴惡，王喜歡當著群臣面前暴惡、生氣、發脾氣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，諸群臣類或餘人等，隨於一處現行少小不如意事，即便對面擯黜，發麤惡言，咆勃忿恚，顰蹙而住，時生憤發。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如有一類國王，諸多群臣或者其他的人，隨在任何一處出現一點點少小不如意的事觸惱國王，國王立刻將他驅擯、罷黜到遠處或邊地塞外去，發出麤惡的言語，暴怒大叫、忿恨、瞋恚，皺眉蹙額愁容滿面，動不動發脾氣。這種國王是當面暴惡型。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、背面暴惡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科背面暴惡，背面向下屬作擯辱等事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">設不對面，背彼向餘而作於前擯辱等事。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　假設不當著大臣等面前擯黜等，也會在當事人背後，在其餘人面前作像前面所說的擯黜等事。這種國王是背面暴惡型。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、懊恚暴惡2　午一、暫時暴惡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科懊恚暴惡，懊惱憤恚的暴惡性，分二科；第一科暫時暴惡，不長時持憤恚心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4907"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">設不對面、亦不背彼向餘而作於前黜罵等事。然唯內意憤恚鬱怏，懷惱害心、懷怨恨心，然不長時持憤恚心相續不捨。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　假設不當著大臣等面前擯黜等，也不在背後，不在其餘人面前作黜罵等事，只是自己私下作黜罵等事，而有懊恚暴惡，這種國王是懊恚暴惡型。或只是內心憤恨不平，鬱鬱不樂。怏，是不滿、不服氣、不快樂的樣子。懷著惱怒傷害的心，懷著哀怨憤恨的心，想要找機會向令他不快樂的對象作報復。但是他這種不好的脾氣及怨恨心不會維持很久，他不會一直想這件事，也不會相續不捨，雖然很生氣，惱火一陣，一下子就放下了。這種國王是暫時暴惡型。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">午二、長久暴惡</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科長久暴惡，長時持憤恚心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有內意憤恚鬱怏，懷惱害心、懷怨恨心，亦於長時持憤恚心相續不捨。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　還有一種國王，內心憤恨不平，鬱鬱不樂，懷惱害心、懷怨恨心，一直放在內心裡面相續不捨。這種國王是長久暴惡型。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、結略義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結略義，要略歸納為立性暴惡。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由如是相對面暴惡、背面暴惡、懊恚暴惡、暫時暴惡、長久暴惡，如是名王立性暴惡。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如上文所說所謂的「立性暴惡」有五種特徵，包括對面暴惡、背面暴惡、懊恚暴惡，暫時暴惡及長久暴惡，其中懊恚暴惡開成兩類，一類是暫時，一類是長久的暴惡，這些可統稱為王立性暴惡。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、出大罪</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科出大罪，顯示屬於長久暴惡的大罪。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">大王當知！長久暴惡名獲大罪，非是餘者。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　大王應當知道！如果國王有長久暴惡的話，他的罪過很大，這是王的最大過失，其他種暴惡還不算是很大的過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅四、猛利憤發</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科猛利憤發，形容瞋心重，於臣等小過重罰。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王猛利憤發？謂有國王，諸群臣等有小愆過、有少違越，便削封祿，奪去妻妾，或以重罰而刑罰之。如是名王猛利憤發。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王猛利憤發？是指有一類國王，諸多大臣們等有小小過失、或有少許違越權責範圍，就將他的薪水削減或拿走了，而且將他的妻妾奪取為己有，或將她配嫁給他人，或以很重的刑罰來處罰他。這種稱為王猛利憤發。這種憤怒一發作起來是很強的，這種王的瞋恨心很重，一點點觸惱都不可以。古時候確實有這種暴君。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅五、恩惠奢薄</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科恩惠奢薄，形容慳吝心重，酬賞過少、苛薄，不能圓滿。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4908"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王恩惠奢薄？謂有國王，諸群臣等供奉侍衛，雖極清淨，善稱其心，而以微劣軟言慰諭；頒賜爵祿、酬賞勳庸不能圓滿，不順常式。或損耗已、或稽留已、或推注已、或怨恨已，然後方與。如是名王恩惠奢薄。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作國王的恩惠奢薄？指有一類國王，下屬們對他供奉侍衛，雖然很清淨，而且很善合他的心意，什麼事都聽國王的話，國王應該要獎賞他們。可是他僅以微劣的，少少一句安慰的話說：還好、還好；並沒有特別獎賞讚歎屬下說：很好、很好。他不會給下屬較高的爵位或很多的薪俸財祿、酬庸嘉賞有功勳的屬下事不能圓滿。例如應該予以記大功，結果王只給他記一個小功，不順常理。「或損耗已」，或者他要給屬下的東西是舊的，或是損耗以後再給屬下；或是該嘉獎、犒賞、贈勳、升官等先拖延一段時間再給，好的獎賞不會馬上給；「或推注已」，或令他受很大的辛勞後才給他，要給對方得個獎，還要他先去某處作什麼事後再給。這就是有一點奢薄，自己很捨不得。或者是遲遲不給對方，直到對方已經開始抱怨憤恨，看到不對勁，對方都快發脾氣了，然後才給。這種國王對下屬的恩惠吝嗇薄情，沒有給下面的人應有的好處，稱為王恩惠奢薄。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》或推注已或怨恨已者：謂或令彼受大劬勞，及或令彼心生怨恨故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是王恩惠奢薄的一種型態，使令對方受到很辛苦的操勞，或是使對方心裡產生怨恨才給予獎賞。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅六、受邪佞言</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科受邪佞言，接受邪執虛假的言論。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王受邪佞言？謂有國王，諸群臣等實非聰叡，有聰叡慢，貪濁偏黨，不閑憲式，情懷謀叛，不修善政，聽受信用如是輩人所進諫議，由此因緣，王務、財寶、名稱、善政并皆衰損。如是名王受邪佞言。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作國王受邪佞言？是指有一類國王，他的群臣等並不是真實的聰明有智，自以為聰明有智，假裝聰明有智的樣子，貪心熾盛，染汙情形嚴重，彼此之間同流合污，相互偏黨，不熟悉法令，謀求背叛國王，不能妥善治理國政，但是國王聽納信受進用這類群臣等所提的不實勸諫提議，由於這類佞臣貪瀆的關係及影響，使得國王的政務、國庫財寶、好的名稱、及過去的善良德政都受到衰損。這類國王不能知人善任，聽受邪佞群臣的諫言，稱為王受邪佞言。佞言，是指不真實的、欺騙的話。閑，是熟悉。憲式是指法令，不閑憲式就是不熟悉法令。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅七、所作不思不順儀則3　卯一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科所作不思不順儀則，國王的作為不經思考不順儀則，分三科；第一科，徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王所作不思不順儀則？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作國王所作所為沒有思惟，而且不順威儀軌則？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋2　辰一、所作不思</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科所作不思，所作沒有仔細思擇觀察。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，不能究察、不審究察、不能思擇、不審思擇諸群臣輩，於彼彼務機密事中，不堪委任而委任之，堪委任者而不委任；堪驅役者而不驅役，不堪役者乃驅役之；應賞賚者而刑罰之，應刑罰者而賞賚之。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　指有一類國王，不能探究觀察、對一般事務不去作一般的觀察與仔細的考察、不能思惟簡擇、不去作周延的思惟簡擇；對於任用的群臣也不能作仔細的思惟簡擇，對於諸事務有顛倒的看法，在各種政務及機密事務中，對所適任的群臣未能適當的委任，對於不適任的卻予以委任；對於可供驅使去辦事的對象不能適當的驅使，對於不能承擔供驅使的對象卻驅使對方去辦事；對於有功應予以獎賞的對象卻予以刑罰；對於有過應予以刑罰的對象卻予以獎賞。這類國王是太差了，沒有頭腦，這也是一個過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4909"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、不順儀則</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不順儀則，不順儀軌法則。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於群臣，不善安處先王儀則；由此群臣處大朝會，餘論未終發言間絕，不敬不憚而興諫諍，不如旨教而善奉行，不正安住王之教命。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種過失的情況是，國王沒有要求群臣遵守先王所設立的王臣朝會的儀式與規則，導致群臣在大朝會中不遵守開會應有的禮儀，其他人的話還沒有說完，臣子就打斷他的話，插嘴發言，對國王既不恭敬也不畏懼，任意提出進諫，繼而諍論。不依國王所下的旨令遵奉執行，也不正確安住於王的教導及命令。這是國王的管理不善，使得群臣不順儀則。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名王所作不思不順儀則。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這樣稱作王所作不思不順儀則。任用臣民的時候，沒有用智慧思惟考察一下，沒有將適當的人放在適當的位置，也沒有要求群臣遵守先王所安立的軌範儀則及君臣禮儀，既無紀律也無效率，加上賞罰不明，使得朝政紊亂，不順儀則。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅八、不顧善法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科不顧善法，不在意、不尊重善法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王不顧善法？謂有國王，不信他世，亦不曉悟；由於他世不信不悟，便於當來善不善業、愛非愛果不能信解；不信解故，無有羞恥，隨情造作身語意業三種惡行，不能時時布施、修福、受齋、學戒。如是名王不顧善法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作國王不顧善法？是指有一類國王，不相信有來生，不相信有後世，也不能覺悟也不能開示群臣；由於不相信有來生，對於所造作的善不善業，來生會感得可愛或不可愛的因緣果報，不能相信、也不能理解；由於對因果不信解的原因，而沒有羞恥心，就為所欲為，任性的造作身語意業三種惡行，也不能時時作好事，如常常布施窮困的人民、修作福報、受持齋戒、修學五戒十善。這種國王不能時時熏修善法，稱為王不顧善法。曉，是開示。悟，是覺悟他人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅九、不知差別忘所作恩3　卯一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科不知差別忘所作恩，不知群臣功過差別，忘記群臣所作恩德，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王不知差別忘所作恩？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作國王不知差別忘所作恩？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋2　辰一、不知差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科不知差別，不知群臣忠信、不忠信等差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4910"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，於諸大臣、輔相、國師及群官等其心顛倒，不善了知忠信、技藝、智慧差別。以不知故，非忠信所生忠信想，於忠信所非忠信想；無技藝所生技藝想，有技藝所無技藝想；於惡慧所生善慧想，於善慧所生惡慧想。彼由如是心顛倒故，於非忠信、無有技藝、惡慧臣所敬重愛養，忠信、技藝、善慧臣所反生輕賤。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是指如有一類國王其心顛倒，對於大臣、輔相、國師、還有群官等不能善巧正確的了知忠誠、信賴、技藝、才華、智慧的差別。由於不知道忠誠信賴等差別相，對於不忠誠、不可信賴者，認為是有忠誠、可信賴，對於忠誠、可信賴者，認為是不忠誠、不可信賴者；對於沒有真實技藝才華者，認為是有真實技藝才華者，有真實技藝才華者，認為是沒有真實技藝才華者；對於有惡慧者認為是良善有智慧者，對於良善有智慧者，認為是有惡慧者。由於心顛倒的原故，對於不忠誠、不可信、沒有真實才藝、有惡慧的臣子等予以恭敬尊重愛護長養，對於真正忠誠可信、有真實技藝、良善有智慧的臣子等反而生出輕賤的想法。這是國王不知道大臣是非善惡的差別，稱為王不知差別忘所作恩。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、忘所作恩</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科忘所作恩，忘饋臣恩。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又諸臣等年耆衰邁，曾於長夜供奉侍衛，知其無勢、無力、無勇，遂不敬愛，不賜爵祿、不酬其賞；設被陵懱，捨而不問。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是說國王忘本，忘記老臣的恩德。又對於有些大臣等已經年老、衰弱、老邁者，他們年輕時曾經長時間的供養侍奉國王，當國王的侍衛，作很多事情，對國家及國王很有貢獻，為國奉獻一生。國王知道他們年邁，沒有威勢、沒有力量、沒有勇氣，不能再作什麼轟轟烈烈的事了，就不再敬愛這些已經退居的老臣，不給他們薪俸（退休金）、爵位、財祿，也不犒賞他們。如果退居的老臣被他人欺陵輕懱了，國王捨棄他們，也不聞不問、不理他們。這種國王忘饋臣恩，稱為忘所作恩。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名王不知差別忘所作恩。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是王的第九種過失，稱作王不知差別忘所作恩。這位國王不知道群臣的差別，並且不能飲水思源，忘本了，忘記曾經給他恩德的這些人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十、一向縱任專行放逸</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科一向縱任專行放逸，一向放縱自己的貪瞋癡於五欲上。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王一向縱任專行放逸？謂有國王，於妙五欲一向沈沒、耽著嬉戲、愛樂受行，不能時時勖勵方便作所應作，勞賚群臣。如是名王一向縱任專行放逸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作國王一向縱任專行放逸？是指有一類國王，對於微妙的色聲香味觸五欲，長時沈沒在其中，耽溺執著嬉笑遊戲，愛樂受用五欲，不能時時勉勵，不能提起精神，精勤作國王應該作的事情，如應該賞賜辛苦的大臣們等，這樣稱作王一向縱任專行放逸。這是第十種作王的過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4911"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、結攝2　寅一、結前</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結攝，結攝十種過失，分二科；第一科結前，結前所說成十過。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有國王成就如是十種過失，雖有大府庫、有大輔佐、有大軍眾，而不可歸仰。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果碰到的國王是有這十種過失，雖然國庫充足、有很多大臣，也有很多軍眾士兵，而是不可以歸投仰靠他。因為有這十種過失，國家必將衰敗，甚至導致滅亡。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、略攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科略攝，要略攝十種過失為二種過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">大王當知！此十過失，初一是王種姓過失，餘九是王自性過失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　大王應當知道！這十種過失：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種是王的種姓過失，就是他受生家世、種姓的過失；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其餘九種是王的自性過失，就是缺少作一個王應有的德行，若是有不得自在、立性暴惡、猛利憤發、恩惠奢薄、受邪佞言、所作不思不順儀則、不顧善法、不知差別忘所作恩、一向縱任專行放逸的九種過失，是名王自性過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、王之功德2　癸一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科王之功德，說明王的功德相，又分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名為王之功德？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王的功德？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、釋3　子一、標成就</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科標成就，標出王成就十種功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">大王當知！王功德者略有十種。王若成就如是功德，雖無大府庫、無大輔佐、無大軍眾，而可歸仰。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛對國王說，你應該知道，王的功德要略而言有十種。如果王成就這十種功德，雖然沒有充足的國庫，也沒有很多有力輔佐的臣子，也沒有很多的軍隊，但卻是可以被眾人所歸投仰靠。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列種類</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列種類，列出十種功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4912"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為十？一、種姓尊高，二、得大自在，三、性不暴惡，四、憤發輕微，五、恩惠猛利，六、受正直言，七、所作諦思善順儀則，八、顧戀善法，九、善知差別知所作恩，十、不自縱任不行放逸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪十種？一、種姓尊高，二、得大自在，三、性不暴惡，四、憤發輕微，五、恩惠猛利，六、受正直言，七、所作諦思善順儀則，八、顧戀善法，九、善知差別知所作恩，十、不自縱任不行放逸。這十種功德，剛好與前面所述的十種過失相反。接著又很詳細的解釋這十種功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、隨別釋2　丑一、辨相10　寅一、種姓尊高</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科隨別釋，各別的解釋，分二科；第一科辨相，說明十種功德的相貌，又分十科；第一科種姓尊高，家族種姓尊貴高尚。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王種姓尊高？謂有國王，處在相似王家而生，宿世尊貴，是相似子。如是名王種姓尊高。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王種姓尊高？是指有一類國王，形貌威儀等與父親相似、人人都很敬愛，對他不會有罵詈傷害的語言，處在相似王家，為皇族所生，從過去世到現在，家世一直都有很尊貴的傳承，是傳承相似尊貴王族之子。這種家世宿世尊貴的國王，稱為王種姓尊高。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、得大自在</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科得大自在，於人於事所作自在。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王得大自在？謂有國王，自隨所欲作所應作，勞賚群臣，於妙五欲歡娛遊戲，於諸大臣、輔相、國師、群官等所，凡出教命，宣布無礙。如是名王得大自在。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王得大自在？是指有一類國王，能夠隨心所欲作應該作的事。能夠賞賜有功勞的群臣，能與大家歡娛遊戲享受五欲，對於大臣、輔相、國師、群官等部屬，凡是王發出宣教或命令，大家都會遵奉執行而沒有障礙，這樣稱作王得大自在。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、性不暴惡2　卯一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科性不暴惡，心性不暴惡，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王性不暴惡？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王的心性沒有暴惡？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋2　辰一、辨差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科辨差別，說明差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4913"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，諸群臣等隨於何處，雖行增上不如意事，性能容忍，不現擯黜，不發麤言，亦不咆勃，廣說乃至不生憤發，亦不背面而作前事，亦不內意祕匿忿纏，亦不長夜蓄怨憤心，相續不捨。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一類國王，若是下面的眾臣不論在什麼地方，雖然作了很多不如國王心意的事，由於國王心量很大，能夠容忍，既不會馬上就驅擯罷黜這類群臣、也不會發出麤惡的語言、皺眉頭、或是生氣大聲說話；不會在背面處理群臣以前發生的事；也不會在內心秘密藏著憤怒的煩惱；更不會長時間相續不捨的蓄積怨恨之心。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、結略義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結略義，結說性不暴惡的要義。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">不現暴惡、不背暴惡、不匿暴惡、不久暴惡。如是名王性不暴惡。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這類國王不現前暴惡、不背面暴惡、不藏匿暴惡、不長久暴惡，剛好與前面所說的暴惡過失相反，顯示國王寬闊的心胸與修養的功德，稱為王性不暴惡。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅四、憤發輕微</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科憤發輕微，指瞋心微小。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王憤發輕微？謂有國王，諸群臣等雖有大愆、有大違越，而不一切削其封祿、奪其妻妾，不以重罰而刑罰之，隨過輕重而行黜罰。如是名王憤發輕微。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王憤發輕微？是指有一類國王，大臣們雖然有大過失，有大違背或超越律法範圍的違犯，國王不會將他所封的臣位及薪俸全部取消，也不會奪走他的妻妾，也不會嚴重處罰他，而是隨對方所犯的過失輕重來執行處罰或罷黜。這類國王是很明理、很厚道的，稱為王憤發輕微。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅五、恩惠猛利</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科恩惠猛利，適時獎賞部屬，廣施恩惠。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王恩惠猛利？謂有國王，諸群臣等正直現前供奉侍衛，其心清淨、其心調順，於時時中，以正圓滿軟言慰諭；具足頒錫爵祿、勳庸，而不令彼損耗、稽留、劬勞、怨恨；易可供奉，不難承事。如是名王恩惠猛利。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王恩惠猛利？是指有一類國王，當群臣等對他真誠現前供奉侍衛時，內心很清淨、又很調柔善順，他能夠常常對這些大臣給以正確、圓滿、柔軟的話來安慰鼓勵他們；能夠適時洽當且圓滿的頒賜給群臣官位、俸祿、功勳、酬庸。不會使令對方應得的獎勵有所損耗；也不會耽誤延遲或使令對方作很多事以後才給；也不會獎賞不公，使令對方心中產生怨恨才給；這類國王很容易供奉承事，很捨得犒賞群臣，稱作王恩惠猛利。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅六、受正直言</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科受正直言，接受正直諫言。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4914"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王受正直言？謂有國王，諸群臣等實有聰叡，無聰叡慢，無濁無偏，善閑憲式，情無違叛，樂修善法，聽受信用如是輩人所進言議，由此因緣，國務、財寶、名稱、善法皆悉增盛。如是名王受正直言。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王受正直言？是指有一類國王，諸多群臣等真實有聰明智慧，也沒有因聰明智慧而高慢，心中沒有貪瞋染污，也沒有偏黨，對法令很熟悉，沒有任何叛逆的想法，好樂修習善法，他能聽受信用這類群臣所進諫的言論。由這樣好的因緣，使得國家的事務、財寶、名稱、善法都能增長強盛，名為王受正直言。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅七、所作諦思善順儀則3　卯一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科所作諦思善順儀則，所作能仔細思考，善順儀則，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王所作諦思善順儀則？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王所作諦思善順儀則？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋2　辰一、所作諦思</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科所作諦思，凡有所作，能仔細究察思擇。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，性能究察、能審究察、性能思擇、能審思擇諸群臣等，於彼彼務機密事中，不堪委任而不委任，堪委任者而委任之；不堪役者而不驅役，堪驅役者乃驅役之；應賞賚者而正賞賚，應刑罰者而正刑罰；凡有所為，審思審擇，然後方作，而不卒暴。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一類國王，生性能探究觀察人事、對所屬的群臣能詳細探究觀察思惟了解、仔細探究思惟決擇後，對於所需交辦的機密事務，對不適當、不能勝任的對象不予委任，能適當、可以委任者才予以委任；不適於擔任供驅役的對象則不會去驅使勞役，能堪供驅使勞役的對象才使其驅使勞役；國王能善識群臣，而且賞罰分明，對於應予以獎賞的群臣能正確而適當適時的獎賞，對應予以懲罰的群臣能正確而適當的懲罰；凡是有所作為，都是審慎思惟決擇然後才作，不會匆忙草率而作決定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、善順儀則</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科善順儀則，凡有所作善順儀則。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於群臣，能善安處先王儀則；由此群臣雖處宴會，終不發言間絕餘論，要待言終，恭敬畏憚而興諫諍，如其旨教而善奉行，能正安住王之教命。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又對於群臣，能夠妥善管理安置他們，遵守過去先王所制訂的禮儀規則；使得眾多群臣雖然處在聚集的議事宴會中，都不會中間打閒岔，等到其他臣子說完，才會次第恭敬而敬畏的提出諫諍之言，國王所說的教化旨令，群臣都能夠妥善遵奉執行，並且能安住在國王的教化薰陶之下。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4915"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名王所作諦思善順儀則。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是稱為王所作諦思善順儀則。也就是王能有智慧觀察思惟決擇，知人善用，妥善管理群臣，善為順從儀則。這是王的第七種功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅八、顧戀善法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科顧戀善法，時時思擇修習善法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王顧戀善法？謂有國王，信知他世；由信知故，便於當來淨不淨業、愛非愛果能善信解；由信解故，具足慚恥，而不縱情作身語意三種惡行，時時思擇布施、修福、受齋、學戒。如是名王顧戀善法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王顧戀善法？是指有一類國王，知道有來生及善因樂果、惡因苦果的道理；由於深信了解因果，對將來由淨業能感得可愛果，由不淨業能感得不可愛果能夠圓滿信順理解；由於信順理解，具足慚愧心及羞恥心，而不會放縱自己的這一念心去造作身語意三種惡行，常常思惟決擇善、惡因果、並能行持布施、修福、受齋、持戒，受持這些善法。這類國王有因果正見，好樂行善，稱為王顧戀善法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅九、善知差別知所作恩3　卯一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科善知差別知所作恩，善知群臣德失差別及所作恩德，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王善知差別知所作恩？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王善知差別，知所作恩？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋2　辰一、善知差別</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科善知差別，善知群臣忠信等差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，於諸大臣、輔相、國師及群官等心無顛倒，能善了知忠信、技藝、智慧差別。若諸群臣忠信、技藝及與智慧，若有若無并如實知。於其無者輕而遠之，於其有者敬而愛之，而正攝受。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如有一類國王，具有智慧的眼光，對於所屬諸大臣、輔相、國師、及群官等的各個能力都能正確而無顛倒的認識，群官等的忠誠、可信、技藝及智慧，具足與否他都如實了知。對於不具備忠信、技藝、智慧的人，國王就遠離這些人，對有具足忠信、技藝、智慧這些條件的人，則很尊敬愛護，也將他們攝受過來當他的大臣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、知所作恩</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科知所作恩，善知群臣昔日所作恩德，分賞無替。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4916"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又諸臣等年耆衰邁，曾於長夜供奉侍衛，雖知無勢、無力、無勇，然念昔恩，轉懷敬愛，而不輕賤，爵祿、勳庸分賞無替。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又對於曾經長久供奉侍衛自己但已經年長力衰、老邁將退休的老臣們，雖然了知他們已經沒有勢力，也不再勇猛了，但是感念他們過去的努力、忠誠效力等恩惠，內心裡面懷著尊敬愛護他們的心情，不會輕賤他們；對所應頒發給他們的官位、財祿、功勳、酬庸等不會漏掉他們，假如有任何好處，總是會想到要分給這些大臣們一分。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結名善知差別知所作恩。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名王善知差別知所作恩。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是王知道群臣的差別，而且知道對於國家或社稷有恩的人，應該要回報恩德，名為王善知差別知所作恩。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅十、不自縱任不行放逸</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科不自縱任不行放逸，不放縱自己於妙五欲，勤於作所應作。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王不自縱任不行放逸？謂有國王，於妙五欲而不沈沒、耽著嬉戲、愛樂受行，能於時時勖勵方便作所應作，勞賚群臣。如是名王不自縱任不行放逸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王不自縱任，不行放逸？是指有一類國王，不會沈溺耽著於五欲與嬉戲玩樂、愛樂受行，能夠時常鼓勵下屬，作為王所應該作的事，對群臣該獎勵就獎勵，該賞賜的就賞賜，王具足這些優點，稱為王不自縱任不行放逸。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、結攝2　寅一、結前</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結攝，結攝成就功德，可作歸仰，分二科；第一科結前，結前所說可作歸仰。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若王成就如是功德，雖無大府庫、無大輔佐、無大軍眾，而可歸仰。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若國王成就這十種功德，雖然沒有豐饒的國庫，沒有很多輔佐的大臣，也沒有很多的軍隊，但這是可以歸依投靠的國王。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、略攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科略攝，要略歸納十種功德為二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">大王當知！如是十種王之功德，初一名為種姓功德，餘九名為自性功德。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　大王應當知道！這十種王的功德，第一種稱作種姓的功德，就是他的家世背景的功德，是沒有辦法改變的，其餘九種是自性功德，是可以不斷改變增上的，是作為一個英明的國王應該具足的功德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬三、王衰損門2　癸一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科王衰損門，國王的衰敗與損壞，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名為王衰損門？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王衰損門？王會衰敗，國家會損壞，這種途徑是什麼？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4917"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、釋3　子一、略說3　丑一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋，分三科；第一科略說，先要略的說明，又分三科；第一科標，標出王衰損有五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">大王當知！王衰損門略有五種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　大王應當知道！王的衰損門要略而言有五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出五種衰損門。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、不善觀察而攝群臣；二、雖善觀察而攝群臣，無恩妙行，縱有非時；三、專行放逸，不思機務；四、專行放逸，不守府庫；五、專行放逸，不修法行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這五種王的衰損門是：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、不善觀察而攝群臣；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、雖善觀察而攝群臣，無恩妙行，縱有非時；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、專行放逸，不思機務；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、專行放逸，不守府庫；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、專行放逸，不修法行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　下面各別解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結說五種王衰損門。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是五種皆悉名為王衰損門。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上這五種都稱為王的衰損門。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、廣釋5　丑一、不善觀察而攝羣臣3　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科廣釋，詳細解釋五種王衰損門，分五科；第一科不善觀察而攝群臣，不能善觀察，而攝受群臣，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王不善觀察而攝群臣？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王不善於觀察而攝受群臣？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、明彼攝</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科明彼攝，說明國王不善觀察而攝群臣的情況。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4918"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，於群臣等不能究察、不審究察、不能思擇、不審思擇，忠信、技藝、智慧差別，攝為親侍，加以寵愛，厚賜爵祿，重賞勳庸，最機密處而相委任，數以軟言現為慰諭。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　指有一類國王，對於所屬群臣的智慧、忠誠可信度、技藝等，不能探究觀察、不去仔細觀察及深入了解、不能思惟簡擇、不去詳細的思惟簡擇。由於識人不明，對於所任用的群臣都當做親信加以寵愛，而且賜予豐厚的爵位與俸祿，重賞獎勵於平庸者，甚至於將最機密事務予以委任對方，還常常以柔軟的話來安慰這些大臣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、成衰損</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科成衰損，成為衰損。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">然此群臣，所付財寶多有損費。若遇怨敵、惡友、軍陣，彼先退敗，恐懼破散為他所勝，遲留人後，奔北無戀，矯行惡策，動虧王政。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　然而這些群臣，對於國王託付的財寶，多半有損失耗費。當國王遇到怨仇敵人、或是惡友、或是敵人陣隊，還未上陣就先喪失勇氣潰散退敗，由恐懼、破膽、驚心無法發揮應負責任，自己躲在後面無法身先士卒，背離國王的寵信，自顧奔走逃逸，這種掩飾的行為和惡劣的策略，虧損國家的政務。為他所勝，不能勝任國家給他的任務。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結說名王不善觀察而攝群臣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名王不善觀察而攝群臣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如是名為王不善觀察而攝受群臣。指國王不懂經濟，也不懂軍事，又不能知人善用，派不適任的大臣掌管經濟，不適任的大臣掌管軍事，擔任邊防重任，導致王政虧損。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、無恩妙行縱有非時3　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科無恩妙行縱有非時，不能適時廣施恩惠，分三科；第一科，徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王雖善觀察而攝群臣，無恩妙行，縱有非時？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王雖然能妥善觀察思擇而攝持群臣，但是卻恆常對有忠信、技藝、智慧的群臣慳吝賞賜，頒賜名位俸祿，即使有要獎賞的時候，已是為時已晚？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、攝2　卯一、明彼攝2　辰一、無恩妙行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科攝，說明所攝，分二科；第一科明彼攝，說明無恩妙行，縱有非時所攝，分二科；第一科無恩妙行，說明無恩妙行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，雖於群臣性能究察、能審究察、性能思擇、能審思擇，忠信、技藝、智慧差別，攝為親侍，而不寵愛，不如其量具賜爵祿，最機密處亦不委任，不數軟言現相慰諭。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　指有一類國王能夠仔細思惟、考察、簡擇屬下的群臣，能夠知道哪些人是有忠信、技藝、有智慧，能進用攝取作為親近侍從。可是他又不懂得愛惜人才，沒有以相應於對方所做的貢獻來賞賜對方爵位與俸祿；對於最機密的事也不信任或委託對方，對方做得很辛苦也有貢獻，也不常常用讚賞鼓勵的話語來慰問對方。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、縱有非時</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科縱有非時，即使有善待屬下時，已是為時已晚，指不能適時施恩。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4919"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">彼於一時，王遇怨敵、惡友、軍陣，廣說乃至大怖畏事命難現前，爾時於臣方行寵愛，廣說乃至數以軟言而相慰諭。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼時候王才會真的重視這些大臣？當王遇到怨仇敵人、或是惡友、或是敵軍乃至有恐怖的事情，有命難要現前或王位不保時，這時對於大臣才開始寵愛，才懂得珍惜這些人才，乃至對他們以柔軟的話來安慰示諭，甚至好言籠絡討好他們。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、成衰損</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科成衰損，成為衰損。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">時群臣等共相謂曰：王於今者危迫因緣，方於我等暫行妙行，非長久心。知此事已，雖有忠信、技藝、智慧，隱而不現。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這時大臣等共同在一起議論，認為：國王只有在很危險，自己已經王位不保的時候，才覺察到群臣們的重要性，才對眾臣們暫時好一點，他不是長久心的。知道這事以後，大臣們將他們的忠信、技藝、智慧，都隱藏起來，也不表現出來。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名王雖善觀察而攝群臣，無恩妙行，縱有非時。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如此名為「王雖善觀察而攝群臣，無恩妙行，縱有非時。」雖然懂得用人，可是該賞賜群臣時，該對群臣好的時候，都沒做；即使再忠誠的部屬也會有怨，長時以往，導致士氣低落，不會真心作事，群臣不會效忠，這是第二種王衰損門。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、專行放逸不思機務3　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科專行放逸不思機務，國王整日在色聲香味觸裡面放逸，不思重要的政務，不作該作的事，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王專行放逸，不思機務？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為國王專行放逸，不思機務？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、舉於應和好方便</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉於應和好方便，舉出應該跟大臣和好方便。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，於應和好所作所成機務等事，而不時時獨處空閑，或與智者共正思惟、稱量、觀察和好方便。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一類國王，對於應該採取親和敦睦的所要作、所要成就的重要的事情，如國防、外交等，不常常在靜處思考，也不與有智慧的人共同正確的思惟、稱量、觀察，尋求執行親和敦睦的方法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、例於乖絕方便等</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例於乖絕方便等，例舉出種種情況下，都不能善用方便。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4920"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是於應乖絕所作所成機務等事，於應惠施所作所成機務等事，於應軍陣所作所成機務等事，於應攝受大力朋黨所作所成機務等事，皆不時時獨處空閑，或與智者共正思惟、稱量、觀察乖絕方便，乃至攝受彊黨方便。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　對於應該斷絕的所作所成機務等事，於應該惠施所作所成的機務等事，於應該布置軍陣所作所成機務等事，於應該攝受有大力量的朋友所作所成機務等事，都沒有時時在靜處獨自思考，或是與有智慧的人，共同正確的思惟、稱量、觀察去推動執行應該斷絕不作的事，乃至攝受強大邦交國的事。做了不該作的事，該作的事沒做，使得國務荒廢。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名王專行放逸，不思機務。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這些都是國家的重要事情，國王忙著色聲香味觸五欲的事，沒有重視機要的政務，很多該作的事情都沒有作，稱為王專行放逸，不思機務。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑四、專行放逸不守府庫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科專行放逸不守府庫，專注在放逸揮霍，沒有看守好國庫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王專行放逸，不守府庫？謂有國王，寡營事業、拙營事業、不持事業、不觀事業，不禁王門、不禁宮門、不禁府庫，或於俳優、伎樂、笑弄、倡逸等所，或復耽樂博弈戲等，非量損費所有財寶。如是名王專行放逸不守府庫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王專行放逸，不守府庫？是指有一類國王很揮霍，不懂得愛惜國庫，不去經營事業，即使經營也很笨拙、沒有善巧、沒有智慧，對已有的事業也不能維繫、運作、繼續保持，也不觀察如何使事業轉好；也不管制王宮大門、府庫，又常常到後宮找人放逸，而後宮大門也是任人隨意進出；國庫有很多錢，他也不懂要節儉，拿來任意揮霍到唱戲的、歌伎、舞樂、嬉笑、滑稽藝人等娼蕩放逸的地方；或者下棋、賭博這些事情，大量的損耗所有的國庫財寶而不節制。這種國王，名為王專行放逸不守府庫。俳優，是古代的滑稽藝人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑五、專行放逸不修法行3　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科專行放逸不修法行，專注於放逸事，而不修善法，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王專行放逸，不修法行？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王專行放逸，不修法行？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、不能諮問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科不能諮問，不能諮詢請問有智之人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4921"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，於世所知柔和淳質、聰慧辯才、得理解脫、巧便無害、樂無害法，所有沙門、若婆羅門，不能數往禮敬諮詢：云何為善？云何不善？云何有罪？云何無罪？作何等業能致吉祥，遠離諸惡？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　指有一類國王，對於世間人共同所知的具有柔和、淳淨、正質的心地、具有聰明智慧口才、知道解脫的道理、善巧無害輔佐國政的方法、好樂無害的善法的出家沙門或有學問的婆羅門等，國王不懂得常常去親近他們，向他們請問及諮詢請益：什麼是善法？什麼是不善法？什麼是有罪？如何作是沒有罪？該作什麼事情，才能夠導致吉祥，遠離種種的災難、惡法？這種國王不知禮遇賢士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、不能修行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科不能修行，不修惠施等善法。</span></span></span></div>
