<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">設得聞已，亦不勖勵如說修行，不能時時惠施、樹福、受齋、學戒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　就算國王聽到出家眾或有學問的婆羅門指導他修善斷惡的方法，他也不如對方所指導的精進、如實修行，不能常常作大布施，樹立福德、受齋、學戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名王專行放逸，不修法行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這稱為王專行放逸，不修法行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、結配2　丑一、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結配，結語配成五種衰損門，又分二科；第一科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有國王成就如是五衰損門，當知此王退失現法、後法義利。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果有國王成就這五種衰損事情的話，當知這位國王就會退失現在的利益、安樂，還會失去來生的利益、安樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科配，五衰損門配成二門。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂前四門退現法利，最後一門退後法利。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面四門，對於：不善觀察而攝群臣、無恩妙行縱有非時、專行放逸不思機務、專行放逸不守府庫這四種事情，在現法當中就會退失現法利益而衰損了，最後的第五種門：專行放逸不修法行，會使他來生受到衰損。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬四、王方便門2　癸一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科王方便門，王的善巧方便門，剛好與王衰損門相反，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名為王方便門？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王方便門？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4922"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、釋5　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分五科；第一科標，標出王方便門有五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">大王當知！王方便門略有五種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛陀告訴王說：大王應該知道！王的施政方便門，要略說有五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為五？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪五種方便門？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列出五種方便門。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、善觀察攝受群臣；二、能以時行恩妙行；三、無放逸，專思機務；四、無放逸，善守府庫；五、無放逸，專修法行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、能善於觀察群臣，攝受有智慧的群臣；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、能在適當的時候，施恩給有貢獻的群臣，這樣群臣對王的恩德有信心，願意恆常忠誠效命，而不改心意；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、身心不放逸在色聲香味觸上，能專心處理國政，令國家安全；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、身心不放逸在色聲香味觸上，會將國庫照顧好，能夠善於經營事業，為國家賺進財富，使老百姓生活富庶；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、不會放逸，常常請問出家及在家的賢善知識，因此懂得如何斷惡修善，使他現在與來生都得到好處。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子四、釋5　丑一、能善觀察攝受羣臣</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋，解釋，分五科；第一科能善觀察攝受群臣，能知人善任。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王能善觀察攝受群臣？謂有國王，於群臣等性能究察、能審究察、性能思擇、能審思擇，忠信、技藝、智慧差別，攝為親侍。如是名王能善觀察攝受群臣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王能善觀察攝受群臣？是指有一類國王，生性能探究觀察、能仔細探究觀察、生性能思惟、能仔細思惟決擇，慎選忠誠可信、有技藝、有才華、有智慧的群臣，作為親近的侍者，這稱作王能善觀察攝受群臣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、能善以時行恩妙行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科能善以時行恩妙行，能適時施恩的妙行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4923"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王能善以時行恩妙行？謂有國王，於諸群臣善觀察已，攝為親侍，加以寵愛，隨其度量厚賜爵祿、重賞勳庸，最機密處而相委任，數以軟言現相慰諭。彼於一時，王遇怨敵、惡友、軍陣，大怖畏事命難現前，即便罄竭，顯示忠信、技藝、智慧。如是名王能善以時行恩妙行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王能善以時行恩妙行？是指有一類國王，對於群臣於善巧的觀察以後，就將忠誠可信、有才華，有智慧的群臣，攝受作為親近的侍者，加以寵愛，隨著群臣貢獻的程度來賞賜對方種種的官位、財祿，有功勳、或有功勞的，他都能夠重重的賞賜。勳，是功勳，較大的功勞；庸，是一般的功勞。對有智慧的臣屬，重要的事情會委託信任他們，跟他們商量，並且常常以讚美的話來鼓勵慰勉這些大臣，讚歎他們作得很好，很辛苦。如果某個時候，國王遇到敵人、或有大怖畏事、或命難現前的時候，這些大臣便會全力以赴，將自己所有的智慧才華、忠信、技藝、智慧完全的貢獻出來，甚至於犧牲生命來拯救大王。這稱為王能善以時行恩妙行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、無有放逸專思機務3　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科無有放逸專思機務，不會放逸，而專心國政，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王無有放逸，專思機務？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王能無有放逸，專思機務？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、舉於和好方便</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉於和好方便，舉出不放逸而專思國防、外交等機務，能成就和好方便。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，於應和好所作所成機務等事，能於時時獨處空閑，或與智者共正思惟、稱量、觀察和好方便。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一類國王，對於應該採取親和敦睦所應作、及所應成就重要、機密的國防、外交等事，能夠常常自己靜下來思考，或者是與有智慧的人，共同思惟、商量、觀察，如何執行親和敦睦的方法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、例於乖絕方便</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科例於乖絕方便，例舉出所不應作的也能不作的方便等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是於應乖絕所作所成機務等事，於應惠施所作所成機務等事，於應軍陣所作所成機務等事，於應攝受大力朋黨所作所成機務等事，皆能時時獨處空閑，或與智者共正思惟、稱量、觀察乖絕方便，乃至攝受彊黨方便。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　國王對於應該斷絕的所作所成機務等事，於應該惠施所作所成的機務等事，於應該布置軍陣所作所成機務等事，於應該攝受有大力量的朋友所作所成機務等事，都能時時在靜處獨自思考，或是與有智慧的人，共同正確的思惟、稱量、觀察去推動執行應該斷絕不作的事，乃至攝受彊大邦交國的事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4924"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名王無有放逸，專思機務。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這樣稱為王沒有放逸，專精思惟機要政務。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑四、無有放逸善守府庫</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科無有放逸善守府庫，不放逸，能善守財庫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王無有放逸，善守府庫？謂有國王，廣營事業、巧營事業、善持事業、善觀事業，善禁王門、善禁宮門、善禁府庫，又於俳優、伎樂、笑弄、倡逸等所，不以非量而費財寶，亦不耽樂博弈戲等。如是名王無有放逸，善守府庫。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王無有放逸，善守府庫？是指有一類國王，很有經濟才華，能夠妥善開源節流，可以廣泛的經營種種各式各樣的國營事業，也能夠很有智慧的經營事業、善於維持事業的正常運作，能夠觀察事業什麼時候該創新轉變，什麼時候該作，知道什麼時候該出門，什麼時候不該出門，什麼時候可以去後宮，什麼時候不要去，時間掌握得很好。對於國庫什麼時候該花，什麼時候不該花，能開源節流、防止貪污作得非常好。國家難免有歌笑舞樂、演戲的事情，但是不會花太多錢在這裡浪費國庫，也不會自己耽著、好樂在下棋、賭博這一類的事情當中。這稱為王無有放逸，善守府庫。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑五、無有放逸專修法行3　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科無有放逸專修法行，不放逸專修善法，分三科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王無有放逸，專修法行？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎麼樣的情況是王無有放逸，專修法行？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、能請問</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科能請問，能請教有聰明智慧的人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，於世所知柔和淳質、聰慧辯才、得理解脫、巧便無害、樂無害法，所有沙門、若婆羅門，而能數往禮敬諮詢：云何為善？云何不善？何等有罪？何等無罪？作何等業能致吉祥，遠離諸惡？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一類國王，對於世間人共同所知具有柔和、淳淨、正質的心地、具有聰明智慧口才、知道解脫的道理、善巧無害輔佐國政的方法、愛樂無害善法的出家沙門或有學問的婆羅門們，國王能常常去親近、禮敬、諮詢，向他們請益：什麼是善法？什麼是不善法？什麼是有罪？什麼是沒有罪？該作什麼事情，才能夠導致吉祥，遠離種種的災難、惡法？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、能修行</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科能修行，能修布施等善行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4925"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">既得聞已，善能勖勵如說修行，亦能時時惠施、樹福、受齋、學戒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　國王去請益以後，又能夠照善知識指導的方法，勉勵自他去做、如實修行，也能夠常常布施、修福、受齋、學戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名王無有放逸，專修法行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這樣稱為王無有放逸，專修法行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子五、結配2　丑一、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科結配，結五方便門，配現法、後法義利，分二科；第一科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有國王成就如是五方便門，當知此王不退現法、後法義利。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如果有國王能夠成就前面所說五種方便門，可知這位國王不會退失現法及後法的利益安樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科配，五方便門配二義利。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂前四門不退現法所有義利，最後一門不退後法所有義利。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　國王能做到前四點，在現法不會退失所有的利益安樂，如果做到最後一點，還懂行善，修福、受齋、學戒，來生也會得到利益安樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬五、王可愛法2　癸一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科王可愛法，說明王的可愛法，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名為王可愛法？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為王可愛法？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、釋4　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分四科；第一科標，標出五種王可愛法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">大王當知！略有五種諸王可愛、可樂、可欣、可意之法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛告訴國王，大王應該知道！要略而言有五種是王可愛的、可樂的、可欣喜的、可意的，內心滿足的法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為五？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪五種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4926"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列出五種王可愛法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、世所敬愛，二、自在增上，三、能摧怨敵，四、善攝養身，五、能往善趣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、世所敬愛，世間人都很敬愛他，當然每個國王都希望受到老百姓的敬愛。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、自在增上，對於人事的安排建立能夠隨意而行，所發佈的命令大家都能奉行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、能摧怨敵，能夠摧滅降伏與己方有怨恨敵意的國家、或是敵人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、善攝養身，能善於保養身體，又很健康。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、能往善趣，來生能夠到人天善趣去。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子四、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是五種，是王可愛、可樂、可欣、可意之法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這五種是王的可愛、可樂、可欣、可意之法。第六科接著說明如何達到。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬六、能引王可愛法2　癸一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科能引王可愛法，說明能引發王的可愛法，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何能引王可愛法？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　怎麼樣才能夠引出國王稱心如意的法？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、釋5　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分五科；第一科標，標出五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">大王當知！略有五種能引諸王可愛之法。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛告訴國王，大王應該知道！要略而說，有五種能夠引發諸國王可愛的法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等為五？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪五種？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科列，列出五種王可愛法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、恩養世間，二、英勇具足，三、善權方便，四、正受境界，五、勤修法行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五種王可愛法是：恩養世間、英勇具足、善權方便、正受境界、勤修法行。由前引後，列出五種，接下來又詳細解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4927"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子四、釋5　丑一、恩養世間2　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科釋，解釋，分五科；第一科恩養世間，王能恩養世間，又分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王恩養世間？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王能夠恩養世間，使得他為世人所敬愛？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、舉正化2　辰一、辨3　巳一、不貪財寶</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉正化，舉出正確教化世間，又分二科；第一科辨，分別三種正化，又分三科；第一科不貪財寶，說明不貪財寶的美德。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，性本知足，於財寶門為性謹慎，不邪貪著，如其所應積集財寶，不廣營求。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一類國王，生性就很知足，對於財寶的取得或積聚，內心很謹慎，不會心生邪念貪取愛著，不是該得的，不會去取得，應該得的才會去積集。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、給施貧窮</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科給施貧窮，布施給貧窮者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有國王，性無貪吝，成就無貪白淨之法，以自所有庫藏珍財，隨力隨能，給施一切貧窮孤露。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有一類國王，本性沒有貪心、也不吝嗇，能成就無貪樂善好施的清淨之法，常常以自己私人的庫藏珍財，隨自己的力量，隨自己所能作的，布施給貧窮、孤苦、無父母照顧的人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、曉諭賞罰</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科曉諭賞罰，如理開導賞罰。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有國王，柔和忍辱，多以軟言曉諭國界；於時時間，隨其所應分賞爵祿；終不以彼非所能業、惡業、重業役任群臣；諸有違犯可矜恕罪，即便矜恕，諸有違犯不可恕罪，以實、以時如理治罰。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有一類國王，性情很柔和，也能夠忍耐他人的羞辱、多數以柔軟好聽、慈悲的話，來開示告誡國人；於時時間，隨大臣們所貢獻的大小，能夠隨他們所應得的來賞賜官位，或者是財祿；不會以大臣們沒有辦法做到，或者是惡業，或者是很重的工作，要求大臣們去做。如果大臣們做出錯誤的事情，是可以憐憫饒恕的罪過，就予以憐憫饒恕。如果所違犯的事情，是不可以饒恕的罪，就以真實的情況，於恰當的時間，如事實的輕重來處罰違犯者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4928"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名王以正化法恩養世間。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這樣稱為王以正確教化的方法恩養世間。國王能以正法來教化，恩養世間，自然會被大臣與百姓所敬愛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋引果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋引果，解釋正化所引果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由王受行如是恩養世間法故，遂感世間之所敬愛。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於王做到不貪財寶、給施貧窮、曉諭賞罰，恩養世間法的三法，會感得世間人的敬愛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、英勇具足2　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科英勇具足，具足英明，勇敢出眾，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王英勇具足？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如何稱為王英勇具足？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、舉英勇</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉英勇，舉出國王英明勇敢事蹟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，計策無惰，武略圓滿；未降伏者而降伏之，已降伏者而攝護之；廣營事業，如前乃至不甚耽樂博弈戲等；</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一類國王，能夠精勤沒有怠惰的策劃國事，國家軍隊精良，武功戰略事業也處理得很圓滿，鄰國還沒有降伏的，能夠去降伏，已降伏的國家，能夠攝受保護他們；能夠廣營事業，如前所說乃至不甚耽樂下棋、賭博、歡娛、戲笑等，前面所說的種種好事都作了；&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》廣營事業如前等者：前說：寡營事業、拙營事業、不持事業、不觀事業，不禁王門、不禁宮門、不禁府庫，或於俳優、伎樂、笑弄、倡逸等所，或復耽樂博奕戲等，非量損費所有財寶。今此翻彼應知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如前面王方便門所說的寡營事業、拙營事業、不持事業、不觀事業，不禁王門、不禁宮門、不禁府庫，或於俳優、伎樂、笑弄、倡逸等所，或復耽樂博奕戲等，非量損費所有財寶等，國王都不會作這些不好的事情，而所作的事情，多為廣營事業、巧營事業等、善持事業、善觀事業、善禁王門、善禁宮門、善禁府庫，增加國家與人民的財富，乃至不會耽樂博奕戲，非量損耗國庫所有財寶等。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4929"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又善觀察應與不應與，勤於僚庶，應刑罰者正刑罰之，應攝養者正攝養之。如是名王英勇具足。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又善能觀察賞賜應不應該給與賞罰，對於臣屬與百姓，應該刑罰的就正確的來處罰之，應該攝取養護的，就攝取養護。這類國王很有智慧、很有理性，能依理而行、如法而行，稱為王英勇具足。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋引果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋引果，解釋所引的果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由王受行如是英勇具足法故，遂能感得自在增上。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於國王深具智慧，不受人情關說的支配，因為無私無貪，能夠適當的支配國家的種種事業，與鄰國的關係也很好，臣子跟民眾的事情也處理得很好，因此能夠感得自在增上的可愛果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑三、善權方便2　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科善權方便，能夠善巧處理事情，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王善權方便？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為王善權方便？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、舉方便</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉方便，舉出和好等方便。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，於應和好所作所成機務等事，如前乃至於應攝受大力朋黨所作所成機務等事，能正了知和好方便，乃至攝受彊黨方便。如是名王善權方便。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一類國王，有善巧、有智慧，應該要作的事情能夠好好的處理，對於應該和好所作所成國防外交機務等事，如前所說乃至應該攝受社會資源、朋友、人力、財力所作所成機務等事，能夠正確知道如何採取親和敦睦的方法，乃至如何採取攝受社會資源、朋友、人力、財力的方法。稱作王善權方便。權，是指處理。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋引果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋引果，解釋所引的結果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由王受行如是善權方便法故，遂能摧伏所有怨敵。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於國王善於治國，所面對的種種事務都能權宜優先次第及輕重緩急，處理得很好，所以與其有怨、有敵對的人，都能夠被其所摧伏攝受。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑四、正受境界2　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科正受境界，正確受用境界，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王正受境界？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作王正確受用境界？</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、舉受用2　辰一、辨2　巳一、列種種</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉受用，舉出受用境界，又分二科；第一科辨，說明，又分二科；第一科列種種，列出種種受用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4930"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，善能籌量府庫增減，不奢不吝，平等自處，清正受用、眾雜受用、勝妙受用、隨其時候所宜受用、與諸臣佐親屬受用、在於勝處而為受用、奏諸伎樂而為受用、無有愆失而為受用。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一類國王，能夠善巧的思惟、觀察考量國庫財富的增加減少，國庫充盈時不奢侈，國庫不足時，該用的花費也不會吝惜。王能夠很合適的處理自己的飲食，能清淨、正確的受用，不同種類的受用，與比較特殊的享受，隨適當的時間，該要受用什麼，能很合適的受用，能與大臣、輔佐、還有親屬等一起共同受用、在殊勝的地方受用，演奏歌舞伎樂使令大家心情放鬆愉快的受用，沒有過失的受用種種飲食，該吃的吃，不該吃的不吃，不多食、不少食、不非量而食。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、釋無愆</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋無愆，解釋沒有過失的受用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">無愆失者，謂疾惱時，應食所宜，避所不宜；於康豫時，消已方食。若食未消，或食而利，皆不應食。應共食者正現在前，不應獨食精妙上味，詭擯餘人。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　沒有過失的受用，是指在有疾病苦惱時，應吃適宜的食物，避免所不宜的食物，以減食為良藥。於病康復痊癒時，前面吃下去的食物要消化後才再吃其它食物，如果吃下去的東西還沒有消化，或者吃下去不能吸收很快就排泄出來，這樣的食物都不應該吃。應該與群臣、百姓共同食用時，會跟群臣、百姓一起共同正確受用這些勝妙的食物，不應該獨自享用美好精妙的食物，詭異驅擯其他人，使他人不得受用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名王正受境界。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這樣稱為王正受境界。主要以受用飲食為例，王能於食知量，有好的食物，大家一起分享，不會將身邊的人遣走，再私下受用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋引果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋引果，解釋所引的善果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由王受行如是正受境界法故，遂能善巧攝養自身。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於王受用食物的時候，很細心注意種種的情況，心情放鬆，還照顧群臣、眷屬，吃的東西不會虛耗府庫，不會每日都十全大補，知道該吃什麼，能正確受用境界，能善巧攝持養護自身，使令自己身體健康。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑五、勤修法行2　寅一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科勤修法行，勤修善法，分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王勤修法行？</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是一位王能夠勤修法行？&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4931"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">寅二、釋2　卯一、舉法行3　辰一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科舉法行，舉出法行，分三科；第一科標，標出法行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂有國王，具足淨信、戒、聞、捨、慧。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有一類國王，具足、圓滿成就對於三寶清淨的信心，受學守持清淨的戒律，聽聞正法、修習惠捨，栽培智慧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰二、釋5　巳一、具足淨信</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分五科；第一科具足淨信，具足信解三世因果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王具足淨信？謂有國王，信解他世，信解當來淨不淨業，及愛非愛果與異熟。如是名王具足淨信。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為王具足淨信？是指有一類國王，相信有來生，而且相信淨業將來會感得可愛的異熟果，不淨業會感得不可愛的異熟果，對於這些事情都很相信，稱作王具足淨信，就是深信因果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳二、具足淨戒</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科具足淨戒，具足受持五戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王具足淨戒？謂有國王，遠離殺生及不與取、婬欲邪行、妄語、飲酒諸放逸處。如是名王具足淨戒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作具足淨戒？有類國王修十善法，遠離殺生、偷盜、欲邪行、妄語、飲酒諸放逸處及貪瞋邪見，不作十惡業，稱作具足淨戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳三、具足淨聞</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科具足淨聞，具足清淨的聞慧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王具足淨聞？謂有國王，於現法義、於後法義，及於現法後法等義眾妙法門，善聽善受，習誦通利，專意研究，善見善達。如是名王具足淨聞。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為王具足淨聞？是指有一類國王，在聽聞佛法的時候，對現在的義利、來生的義利、以及於現在與來生都有義利的事，種種微妙的法門，能夠很專注、很圓滿的聽聞、領受，不斷的學習、讀誦直到通達明利，專心研究，善於觀察及通達所聽聞的法義，這樣稱為王具足淨聞。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳四、具足淨捨</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科具足淨捨，具足清淨的布施。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4932"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王具足淨捨？謂有國王，雖在慳垢所纏眾中，心恆清淨，遠離慳垢，而處居家常行棄捨，舒手樂施，好興祠福，惠捨圓滿，於布施時常樂平等。如是名王具足淨捨。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為王具足淨捨？是指有一類國王，雖然處在有慳貪、有煩惱所纏繞的大眾當中，心裡恆常保持清淨，遠離慳貪的煩惱；能以在家的身分，常行布施、棄捨財物，親手布施，喜歡發動祭祀、供養三寶、培養福報，布施圓滿，於布施時，常常歡喜平等普施。能做到這樣稱為王具足淨捨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">巳五、具足淨慧</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科具足淨慧，具足清淨的智慧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何名王具足淨慧？謂有國王，如實了知善不善法、有罪無罪、修與不修、勝劣黑白，於廣分別諸緣生法亦如實知；縱令失念，生惡貪欲、瞋恚、忿、恨、覆、惱、慳、嫉、幻誑、諂曲、無慚、無愧、惡欲、惡見，而心覺悟，并不堅住。如是名王具足淨慧。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為王具足淨慧？指有一類國王，能夠如實了知善不善法、不善法是有罪的，善法是無罪的、有沒有修行的差別、欲界是下劣，色無色界是殊勝的、有罪的黑業是或者是無罪的白業，能廣大詳細分別十二緣生諸法，也能如實了知緣生諸法；假使一時失去正念，生起惡心、貪欲、瞋恚、忿怒、結恨、覆藏、惱怒、慳貪、嫉妒、虛幻欺誑、諂媚歪曲、無慚、無愧、惡欲、惡見等，馬上能正知，能夠醒覺曉悟，不會一直陷在這些染污煩惱心所裡面。這樣稱為王具足淨慧。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辰三、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是名王勤修法行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這稱作國王能夠精進的修行佛法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">卯二、釋引果</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋引果，解釋所引的果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由王受行此法行故，能往善趣。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　由於王能常常注意因果事，也如實的了知緣生法，恆常修五戒十善，將來能夠到人天的善趣受果報。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子五、結配2　丑一、結</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科結配，結語配釋兩種利益，分二科；第一科結，結語。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">如是五種能引發王可愛之法，能引諸王現法、後法所有利益。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面所說的五種能夠引發王可愛的法，能使國王得到現在世，或是來生所有的利益安樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4933"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科配，五種王可愛的法配為兩種利益。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂初四種能引發王現法利益，最後一種能引發王後法利益。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前面說的恩養世間、英勇具足、善權方便、正受境界等四種，能夠引發國王現法的利益，最後一種勤修法行，能夠引發國王後法的利益。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛三、結勸3　壬一、總勸修學</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科結勸，結語勸國王要這樣修，分三科；第一科總勸修學，總勸修學功德等法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，大王當知！我已略說王之過失、王之功德、王衰損門、王方便門、王可愛法，及能引發王可愛法，是故大王應當修學。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛陀開示完以後，對國王說：大王應當知道！我已經要略的說明作國王的過失、作國王的功德、還有怎麼樣會使令國王衰敗損害，作國王的方法、作國王的可愛法，以及能夠引發王的可愛法，因此大王應該好好的修學。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、別勸所宜</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別勸所宜，各別勸說應該要作什麼。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">王之過失宜當遠離，王之功德宜當修習，王衰損門宜當遠離，王方便門宜當修學，王可愛法宜當希慕，能引發王可愛之法宜當受行。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　佛陀再作一個結語：王的過失應該要遠離，王的功德應該要修習，王的衰損門應該要遠離，王的方便門應當要修學，王的可愛法應該要希望仰慕，能夠引發王可愛的法應該去實踐受行。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬三、明獲利樂</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科明獲利樂，說明如說修行，當獲一切利益安樂。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">大王若能如是修學，當獲一切利益安樂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　大王，如果能夠照著這樣修學，現在可獲得利益，將來可獲得種種的安樂。在經文中說，佛陀說完以後，還勸告國王說：如上所說教導王的這些法，是秘密的王教，依之修行即名聖王，即名法王。國王，如果每日早晨都將這一段經文拿起來讀一讀，而且照著作，就稱作聖王，也稱作法王。國王如果能依教奉行，會感得諸佛菩薩、天龍八部，日夜加持，恆常護念；風調雨順，戰爭都沒有了，兵革止息；各國都會來進貢，不用去進貢他人，所得的福報無量無邊，作國王的時間也會無量無邊；國家安定，國土安寧，壽命長遠。以上說明如何作一個好國王，到這裡作一個結束。這是「引經說」，前一段是《出愛王經》，就是《佛為優填王說王法政論經》。現在是引《八苦經》而說。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">己二、決擇諸苦諦相差別2　庚一、別辨八苦7　辛一、生苦2　壬一、徵</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科決擇諸苦諦相差別，決斷簡擇諸苦諦相的差別，這是引《八苦經》所說，《八苦經》又名《佛說五王經》，或《佛說五王八苦經》，分二科；第一科別辨八苦，各別說明八苦，又分七科；第一科生苦，說明生的苦，又分二科；第一科徵，提問。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;"><a name="17259:49117"></a><a name="65037:49117"></a><a name="34728:49117"></a><a name="22975:49117"></a><a name="43587:49117"></a><a name="28718:49117"></a><a name="1625:49117"></a>復次，如說生苦，乃至略說五取蘊苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，如是說生苦等八苦，要略歸納即是五取蘊苦，五蘊由取而來，又依五蘊生取，實是一切苦的所依。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、釋2　癸一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋，解釋，分二科；第一科標列，標示列出生苦五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4934"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何生苦？當知此苦由五種相。謂眾苦所隨故，麤重所隨故，眾苦所依故，煩惱所依故，不隨所欲離別法故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼是生苦？應當知道生苦由五種相貌所顯示。包括眾苦所隨故，麤重所隨故，眾苦所依故，煩惱所依故，不隨所欲離別法故。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、隨釋5　子一、眾苦所隨故苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨釋，接著各別解釋，分五科；第一科眾苦所隨故苦，說明眾苦所隨故苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何眾苦所隨故苦？謂生那落迦及一向苦餓鬼趣中，若於胎生、卵生生時，種種憂苦之所隨逐，故名眾苦所隨故苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為眾苦所隨故苦？是由苦惱的果報說生為苦，如生到地獄去，或者生一向是苦的餓鬼趣當中，不是有福德的鬼，包括一部分的畜生也是一樣，或者是胎生、或者是卵生，生的時候會有種種的憂苦之所隨逐，稱作眾苦所隨故苦。這是指苦惱的果報而言，《雜集論》說這是屬於異熟障麤重，在地獄或一向是苦的餓鬼趣，無論是胎生或是卵生，出生之後唯苦無樂，而且有眾多苦，因此稱生為眾苦所隨故苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、麤重所隨故苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科麤重所隨故苦，煩惱品種子的麤重所隨故苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何麤重所隨故苦？謂三界諸行，為煩惱品麤重所隨，性不調柔，不自在轉，由此隨逐三界有情諸行生起，故名麤重所隨故苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為麤重所隨故苦？主要是指煩惱等麤重（種子）隨逐於心故，說生為苦。有情於三界果報有為諸法，有煩惱種子隨逐在阿賴耶識中，使心剛強不調柔，不能隨意自在，因此煩惱種子隨逐三界有情的心心所法生起，使心無堪能性斷除煩惱、成就聖道，這些都是從生而來，所以說生是麤重所隨故苦。麤重是一種繫縛，經論中說麤重有四種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、現行有漏諸心心所。《雜集論》說有24種:</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　1、一切遍行戲論麤重者，指執眼等諸法習氣，無始時來依附阿賴耶識相續不斷，名為戲論習氣，從此習氣眼等諸法及名言執數數生起。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　2、領受麤重者，指有漏諸受習氣。（未斷根本我執煩惱相應之三受）</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　3、煩惱麤重者，指煩惱隨眠。（煩惱種子）</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　4、業麤重者，指有漏業習氣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　5、異熟麤重者，指異熟無堪能性。（果報上的無堪能性）</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　6、煩惱障麤重者，指猛利長時煩惱性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　7、業障麤重者，指能障道無間等業障性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　8、異熟障麤重者，指與諦現觀相違，地獄等自體得。（三惡道果報）</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　9、蓋麤重者，指能障礙善品方便盛貪欲等性。（五蓋）</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　10、尋思麤重者，指能障礙欣樂出家欲尋思等性。（欲恚害等八種尋思）</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　11、飲食麤重者，指極多少食於方便行無堪任性。（食不知量障礙修止觀）</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　12、交會麤重者，指兩兩形交身心疲損性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　13、夢麤重者，指睡眠所發身惛劣性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　14、病麤重者，指諸界互違所發不安隱性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　15、老麤重者，指大種衰變所起不隨轉性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　16、死麤重者，指臨命終時諸根亂性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　17、勞倦麤重者，指遠行等所作支體頓弊性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　18、堅固麤重者，指無涅槃法者，如其所應，所有戲論麤重等性。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　19、麤麤重者，指欲界所有麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　20、中麤重者，指色界所有麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　21、細麤重者，指無色界所有麤重。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　22、煩惱障麤重者，指聲聞獨覺菩提所治。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　23、定障麤重者，指九次第定所發功德所治。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　24、所知障麤重者，指一切智性所治如是隨其所應。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、現行二障，指現行煩惱障和所知障</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、二障種子，指煩惱障和所知障種子。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、二障習氣，指煩惱障和所知障習氣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　詳細分別麤重有很多種，這裡特別指煩惱種子隨逐於身引發的苦惱。&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、眾苦所依故苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科眾苦所依故苦，衰老等眾苦所依故苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何眾苦所依故苦？謂衰老等眾苦差別之所依故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱為眾苦所依故苦？這是由苦的現行故，說生是苦，因為老病死、愛別離、怨憎會、求不得等種種苦都是依止五蘊而生，如果沒有五蘊生，就沒有這些苦，因此說生是眾苦所依。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子四、煩惱所依故苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科煩惱所依故苦，對於愛境愛等煩惱所依故苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何煩惱所依故苦？謂受生已，於愛境愛，於瞋境瞋，於癡境癡，由是因緣，住不寂靜惛蕩身心不安隱苦，故名煩惱所依故苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作煩惱所依故苦？這是由煩惱所依故，說生為苦，在三界受生以後，因為不知道一切法都是內心的分別，對於可愛的境界生起愛著，對於令心瞋怒的境界生起瞋心，對於令心愚癡的境界會有愚癡產生，由於這些因緣，內心永遠不能寧靜，總是有很多的煩惱引發身心種種不安隱的苦。這些苦惱都從生而來，因此稱生為煩惱所依故苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4935"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子五、不隨所欲離別法故苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科不隨所欲離別法故苦，生者皆會死故苦。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何不隨所欲離別法故苦？謂諸有情生者皆死、生必殞歿，所有壽命死為邊際、死為終極，如是等事非其所愛，由此因緣，唯受眾苦，是以不隨所欲離別法故，說生為苦。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作不隨所欲離別法故苦？這是由死故，說生為苦，只要生、不要死，好生惡死，一切眾生都是這樣。所有的有情，有生就有死、有生必定會死，所有的壽命，死為邊際、死為終極，這些事情不是眾生有情所喜歡的，由此死歿因緣，領受眾多苦惱，不隨自己的希望遠離所愛的五蘊，這種離別法性，從生而來，因此說生就是苦。除了阿羅漢入無餘涅槃，不再到三界受生才沒有苦，只要到三界受生一定還有苦。雖一時沒有煩惱的現行，仍有煩惱的種子，終究會碰到苦，而且死苦最難忍受，所有的親屬財富等都要放棄，平常好好的時候覺得好像不怕死，真要死的時候，要到最後一口氣，恐怕會很不習慣，雖然已經死過很多次了，也會捨不得。這是說生苦。此處再作一個決擇。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛二、老苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科老苦，說明老苦有五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何老苦？當知亦由五相。謂於五處衰退故苦。一、盛色衰退故；二、氣力衰退故；三、諸根衰退故；四、受用境界衰退故；五、壽量衰退故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作老苦？老苦也有五個相貌，在五種處所有衰老敗退的現象，所以很苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、盛色衰退，美好的容色由光澤明亮到髮白面皺，自已看了都難以忍受，所以世間人開設美容醫院，發明種種保養品，企圖挽救已逝的青春。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、氣力衰退，老的時候精氣體力都不再飽滿充足，不能像年輕時滿身是勁，有時連一碗飯都端不起來。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、諸根衰退，老的時候六根不再靈敏，兩眼昏花、兩耳重聽、鼻不知香臭、舌根不識美味，身根反應不敏捷，意根更是念慧衰退，更嚴重者還患上老人癡呆，迷迷糊糊，自他難辨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、受用境界衰退，再也不能春天去郊遊，夏天去游泳等受用世間美好的境界，去唱歌、跳舞，聲音已是不一樣，如年輕人到處吃喝玩樂，都不能了。每個人到老時都會碰到，必定有這種苦。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、壽量衰退，這件事更苦，過一日少一日，六十歲以後一年不如一年，七十歲以後一個月不如一個月，八十歲以後一日不如一日，九十歲以後一小時不如一小時，頂多到百歲就準備要掛在牆上。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》謂於五處衰退故苦等者：此中五相，如本地分說老差別，隨應當知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/10.htm#49134:7177">陵本十卷二頁732</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此中五種衰退相貌，如前面〈本地分〉卷10，304頁生雜染中所說的老差別，應當知道。前文所說老苦還有很多種，包括身老、心老、壽老、變壞老、自體轉變老等。《涅槃經》說老苦：「譬如燈炷唯賴膏油，膏油既盡勢不久停」。人也一樣，壯年如膏，壯膏既盡，衰老之炷怎能久住？又《出曜經》佛說老苦偈：「少時意盛壯，為老所見逼，形衰極枯槁，氣竭憑杖行」。《雜集論》說老也是一種麤重，障礙種種美好之事，障礙修道，老真是苦！</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛三、病苦</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科病苦，說明病苦五相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">云何病苦？當知病苦亦由五相。一、身性變壞故；二、憂苦增長多住故；三、於可意境不喜受用故；四、於不可意境非其所欲彊受用故；五、能令命根速離壞故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　什麼稱作病苦？病苦也有五相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、身性變壞故，身體變瘦等，美好的形相被破壞了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、憂苦增長多住故，有病的時候，憂愁苦惱增長。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、於可意境不喜受用，對於可愛的境界不歡喜受用故。比如說感冒時，鼻根不靈，很香的東西聞起來也不會覺得香，生病時沒有力氣受用喜歡、可愛的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、於不可意境非其所欲彊受用故，如說吃藥、開刀，這些不可愛的境界沒有人喜歡，當病非得開刀，非得吃藥，還是得勉強受用，這件事相當苦。</span></span></span></div>
