<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、第二語</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二語，第二種說話的方式：愛似非愛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有語言辭句勃逆，然是所宜，是第二語。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者對方說這句話，聽起來好像很兇暴，很違背、忤逆自己的喜好，可是對自己是很合適，剛好可以提升自己。比如說，老師罵一句：怎麼可以將手放在頭上？這句話聽了令人不悅，但是出於善意，能改正自己的威儀。又如父母對孩子破口大罵時，心裡是很愛護孩子，希望孩子轉好。父母愛孩子，師長責罰弟子，都是這種情況。或者禪師為了刺激弟子，對也三十棒、錯也三十棒，對也罵、錯也罵。這樣子來調教弟子，是為了使令弟子與法相應，動機是好的，是為了提升弟子，可是表現出來的語言行動讓弟子不高興，不隨順弟子，違背、忤逆弟子的心情。「愛似非愛」，是指動機是好的，可是表達的方式使人受不了。這是第二類語言。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、第三語</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科第三語，第三種說話的方式：非愛似非愛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有語言辭句勃逆，亦非所宜，是第三語。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　或者有的語言辭句忤逆違背對方的心意，不隨順對方，說的話也很尖銳，純粹是為了罵人，動了瞋心口出惡語，這種是非愛似非愛，心裡並不是愛護對方，說出來的話也令人不舒服，這種是第三類的語言。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸四、第四語</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科第四語，第四種說話的方式：愛似愛。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4950"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有語言辭句善順，亦是所宜，是第四語。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是最好的，心裡很愛護對方，也希望對方成長，說的話又很柔軟，很善順，很美好，使人聽了很舒服，又很隨順對方的心裡，對方又能夠改正自己的錯誤。這樣的語言大家都喜歡，像春風拂面，聽起來也沒有什麼強烈的震擊，可是受教者內心會知道，馬上警覺到，就像良馬能夠見鞭影而行，鞭子輕輕地一舉起來，就知道往前走了。這種語言是最好，最巧妙，這是第四類語言。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬三、別配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科別配，各別配釋三士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">若有宣說非愛似非愛、非愛似愛語者，是下士；若有宣說愛似非愛語者，是中士；若有宣說愛似愛語者，是上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　若有人內心動機不是愛，表達的方式也是不可愛、令人受不了的話；或是心不愛護對方，表達的方式卻是可愛的好話，口蜜腹劍，這是下士。第二種人其實很愛護對方，內心是為了要對方好，不過出口比較粗暴，聽起來讓人不喜歡聽，覺得很刺耳，這是中品的語言，是中士。最高明、最好的，說的話是愛語，能夠提升聽者向善向上，是真實愛護眾生的心情，所說的話讓聽者覺得像春風拂面一樣，眾生都喜歡這種境界，這然是上品的，上士的語言。只有佛菩薩才能夠知道何時應該說苦切語，或是應該說可愛語，要觀眾生的根器來說話。不是每個人都適合接受軟言美語，有些人呵斥一聲，從此變得更好；有些人是欠罵的，有些人是欠鼓勵的，每個人根性不同，佛菩薩能應機說教，知道對眾生什麼時候應該說什麼話，才能真實令眾生獲得利益安樂。以上是約語言來分下中上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛八、約受用諸欲辨3　壬一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第八科約受用諸欲辨，約受用諸欲分辨三士，分三科；第一科標，標出三種受欲者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有三種受諸欲者。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　還有三種受用諸欲的人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、列3　癸一、第一人</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三種受欲者，分三科；第一科第一人，非法受欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有受欲，非法孟浪積集財寶，不能安樂正養己身及與妻子，廣說乃至不於沙門、婆羅門所修殖福田。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人受欲的人，用不合法、魯莽的方法積集財寶，不能安樂正確長養己身及妻兒子女，自己都得不到安樂，更何況妻兒等；也不懂得對出家的沙門、有學問的婆羅門行布施、修福、供養等福業事。這是第一種受欲的人。前面曾說過《中阿含經》中說有十種受欲者，在〈本地分‧意地〉卷3，98頁性類差別的善法中有提過。這是第一種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、第二人</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二人，第二種人，法或非法受欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有受欲，法或非法、孟浪或非積集財寶，能以安樂正養己身、妻子、眷屬及知友等，不於沙門、婆羅門所修殖福田。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種受欲的人，以合法或不合法，魯莽或不魯莽的方法積集財寶。賺了錢，得到欲時能夠使自己平安快樂，也能夠長養自己的妻子兒女，使令眷屬也能夠獲得利益安樂，乃至能夠跟朋友分享，但是對出家的沙門、有學問的婆羅門沒有行布施，也不去供養，只是將自己、眷屬及朋友照顧得很好，一起受用諸欲。這是第二種受欲的人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、第三人</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科第三人，第三種人，如法受欲。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4951"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">或有受欲，一向以法及不孟浪積集財寶，能以安樂正養己身，廣說乃至能於沙門、婆羅門所修殖福田。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人，一向是以合法及不魯莽的方式，規規矩矩的積集財寶；所賺的錢，不會粗心大意，隨便亂用，是很有智慧在受用這些欲，能夠自己受用，也能夠給妻子兒女受用，也願意給朋友受用，也能夠對出家的沙門、有學問的婆羅門行布施，也能夠修福，這樣的人是另一種受欲的型態。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬三、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科配，再以積集財寶與運用的方式配釋上中下三士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">此三種中，初名下士，次名中士，後名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人是最不好的，是非法孟浪積集財寶，以不合道理，而且以很魯莽的方法獲得這些財物，又不能安樂正養自己，也不長養妻子兒女，更不布施修福，這種受欲者是下品的下士。另外一種人有時以合法，有時以不合法的方式積集財寶，也能夠使令妻子兒女跟朋友一同享受欲樂，可是不布施修福，這是中品的中士。第三種人以合法、不魯莽、不粗暴的方式積集財寶，能夠安樂正確長養自己、妻子兒女、朋友，乃至能夠布施、修福，用來修行，這種人是上品的上士。共分成這三類人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛九、約受用飲食辨3　壬一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第九科約受用飲食辨，以受用飲食分辨三士，分三科；第一科標，標出三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有三人。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　還有另外三種人，是約受用飲食的方式來說明。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、列3　癸一、第一人</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出受用飲食的三種人，分三科；第一科第一人，第一種人，貪染而食。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、有人貪染而食，愛著、饕餮乃至耽湎，不見過患、不知出離。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人，貪心染著受用飲食，對於飲食十分愛著、貪得無厭，吃的時候很貪心，吃完了還想帶著走，耽溺沈湎在好的食物裡面，不知道貪吃、吃太多也會有種種的壞處，不知道出離貪食的煩惱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　古神話說：饕餮是一種貪殘的惡獸，有頭無身，後來的人就引喻貪財稱作「饕」，貪吃稱作「餮」。現在人引喻所有貪吃的人，都稱作饕餮。在語言上有些演變。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、第二人</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二人，第二種人思擇而食，於此食未斷未知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">二者、有人思擇而食，不染不著，亦不饕餮、吞吸、迷悶、堅住、耽湎，深見過患，善知出離，而於此食未斷未知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種是修行人，經過思惟簡擇之後才受用飲食，不會飢不擇食，為了大悲心而吃素，不執著食物，不會貪吃，受用飲食時，不會迫不及待的樣子，不會迷惑，不會憂愁，不會將心全部放在食物上執著而不知道出離，也不會耽溺沈湎在好的食物上；能知道貪食會有種種的過失災患產生，因為藉由段食長養六根及心心所，增益悅意觸食及意思食，由此三食滋潤識食，使得生死輪轉不休，已能知道應當出離貪食、貪心的過患、貪心的種子；但是道力不足，還沒有辦法在定裡修觀，不能證得諸法實相，只是調伏貪食的煩惱，不能正知貪食的煩惱種子還未斷除，不是真實知道貪食的過患。不過，已經能夠調伏自己，因為已經有思擇力了。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、第三人</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科第三人，第三種人思擇而食，於此食已斷已知。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">三者、有人思擇而食，不生貪染，廣說乃至深見過患，善知出離，又於此食已斷已知。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人能思惟簡擇而食，不會生貪心染著，能深見貪食的過失災患，知道四食使眾生輪迴生死，知道出離食的過患，受用食物完全為了修行，已經斷除貪煩惱種子，真正如實知道貪食的過患，是得聖道的人。這是第三類人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又貪食是屬於修惑所攝，若約聖人斷見惑與修惑差別，也可相對說，第二種人是初果聖人，第三種是三果以上聖人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4952"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬三、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科配，再以貪食、出離食、斷貪食種子配釋上中下三士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初名下士，次名中士，後名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人是一般人，是下品的下士；第二種人是修行人，已知道食的過患了，不再染著，可是還沒有斷除煩惱種子，這是中品的中士；第三種人是得聖道了，已經斷除貪食的煩惱種子，而且也知道食的過患，這是上品的上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛十、約施戒修辨3　壬一、施所攝3　癸一、依施物建立3　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第十科約施戒修辨，約布施、持戒、修福來說明三士，分三科；第一科施所攝，說明布施所攝三士，分三科；第一科依施物建立，依所施的物品建立三士，分三科；第一科標，先標出依施物說三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復依施物說有三人。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依止所布施的物品來說，有三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、有人所施之物，但具妙香，不具美妙味之與觸；二者、有人所施之物，具妙香味，而無妙觸；三者、有人所施之物，具足美妙香味與觸。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人，有人所布施的物品，只有具足美妙香味，但沒有很美妙的味道，接觸時也不是那麼柔軟、細滑、舒服。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種人，所布施的物品，有微妙的香，也有微妙的味道，吃起來也很好，但是沒有妙觸，身根接觸到的時候不會覺得很舒服。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人，所布施的物品，具足美妙的香、味、觸，柔軟度也很夠，除了有美妙的香，味道很好，香氣很好，也很柔軟。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科配，再以布施物品的香、味、觸之具足與否來配釋上中下三士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初名下士，次名中士，後名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人所布施的物品，只有美妙的香氣，沒有美味，也沒有美好柔軟的觸，稱作下士。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種人所布施的物品，有美妙的香與味，但沒有柔軟的觸，這是中士。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人所布施的物品，同時具有美妙的香、味、觸，這是上士。以上是約布施的物品來建立三士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、依施田建立2　子一、標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依施田建立，約所布施的福田來說明三士，分二科；第一科標列，標示列出依施田說有三人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又依施田說有三人。一者、有人於愛於恩而行惠施；二者、有人於貧苦田而行惠施；三者、有人於具功德最勝福田而行惠施。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又約所布施的福田來說，有三種人：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人，對所喜愛的妻子兒女，及對己有恩的父母師長，能夠施行恩惠布施。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種人，對於貧苦的眾生，有病的、有苦的眾生，施行布施。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人，對於具足聖道功德及最勝福田之三寶處能夠施行布施。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4953"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、別配2　丑一、第一義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別配，各別配屬三士，分二科；第一科第一義，約第一種道理來說三士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初名下士，次名中士，後名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種布施者是下品的下士；第二種是中士；第三種是上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、第二義</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科第二義，約第二種道理來說三士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復有差別。施於所愛名為下士，施於有恩名為中士，施於貧苦、具德勝田名為上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有不同的道理說明三士。布施給所喜歡的人，容易做得到，是下士。布施給於己有恩的人，知道感恩，這種人是中品的中士。布施給貧苦的人，對方真的很需要這些財物，能做應時布施，還有布施給具足聖道功德及最勝福田之三寶處，稱作上士。這是兩種分類法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、依施心建立3　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科依施心建立，約布施時的心念、意樂來建立三士，分三科；第一科標，標出依施心說有三人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又依施心說有三人。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又布施的時候心念也不斷的運轉，依布施時的心念說有三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出依施心的三人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、有人將欲惠施，先心歡喜，正惠施時心不清淨，惠施已後尋復追悔；二者、有人先心歡喜，施時心淨，施已追悔；三者、有人先心歡喜，施時心淨，施已無悔。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種，有人想要布施以前，心裡很歡喜，真正要將錢或食物拿出來時，又有點捨不得，所以不清淨，布施以後還有一點後悔。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種，有人布施以前很高興，布施時心裡很清淨，布施以後，就開始後悔了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種，還沒有布施以前很高興能作這種布施的功德，深切的了解今日自己有能力，才能夠修布施的功德，如果今日自己很貧苦，就變成要被布施的對象，能夠布施表示自己也有一點善業，才會有這種福報可以作這件事；布施的時候，心裡很清淨，也很恭敬，沒有一點捨不得的狀況產生，也不會輕懱他人，不認為對方是接受自己布施的人；布施以後就不會再追念後悔這件事，因為布施這種事，能使令自己功德圓滿，福德增長，這是第三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科配，再以布施時的心念來配釋上中下三士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初名下士，次名中士，後名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人是下品的，本來很高興，可是布施時又有點猶豫，布施以後又後悔了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種人是中士，布施以前很高興，布施時心也清淨，也能夠很謙虛的布施，但布施以後又後悔了，這是中士。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人，不但布施以前滿心歡喜；布施時，心裡很清淨、很誠懇，布施以後也不會再後悔，這是上士。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是約所布施的物品、所布施的福田對象、布施的心情來分辨下中上三品人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4954"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、戒所攝7　癸一、依福業事建立2　子一、總標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科戒所攝，約持戒的情況來辨明三士，分七科；第一科依福業事建立，依福業事建立三士，又分二科；第一科總標，總相標出於受持戒福業事建立三人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復於受持戒福業事建立三人。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又依受除淨戒的福業事，也可以建立三種人。持戒能遠離惡法，內心清淨獲得今生的快樂及來世快樂的果報，名持戒福業事。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列配，列出三種受持淨戒福業事配釋三士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、有人但離一分，非一切時常能遠離，唯自遠離，不勸他離，亦不讚美，見同法者心不歡喜，是名下士。二者、有人離一切分，一切時離，唯自遠離，不勸他人，亦不讚美，見同法者心不歡喜，是名中士。三者、有人一切俱現，是名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種持戒修福的人，只有遠離一分不善，只持一部分的戒，不是全部受持，某一些戒能持，某些戒不能持；也並不是一切時常能遠離惡法；而且持戒只是自己持，看到他人行惡法不作持戒福業事的時候，也不會勸他人遠離惡法；他人真的有持戒福業事，不能讚歎，心裡也不高興，可能有比較的心情，有一種嫉妒的心情；看到同受戒者作持戒福業事時，也不懂得隨喜，這種人稱作下士，是持下品戒者。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種持戒修福的人，一切不善的部分都能夠遠離，因為持戒是要制惡，能夠完全遠離不善；而且不是偶而持，是一切時都是持戒清淨；但是只有自己遠離惡法；不會勸他人來持戒修福；也不讚美他人持戒修福；見到同受戒者持戒修福，心裡也不是很高興，這是中士。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人是最好的，自己完全具足持戒清淨福業事，完全遠離不善；能夠勸他人也持戒修福；看到同受戒者持戒修福，也非常的歡喜讚歎；這種人有隨喜功德，又沒有嫉妒心，這種人是上士。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這段文可以參考卷53，1747頁，由百行所攝而受律儀，「約少分遠離、多分遠離、全分遠離」；「少時遠離、多時遠離、盡壽遠離」；「唯自遠離，勸他遠離」；「稱讚遠離、慶悅遠離」等十種，說明持戒得福的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、依禁戒處所建立3　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依禁戒處所建立，約出家人受持禁戒來分三士，分三科；第一科標，標出三人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於受持禁戒處所建立三人。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又於受持禁戒的作法不同建立三品人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三種受持禁戒者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、有人住惡說法毗奈耶中受持禁戒；二者、有人住善說法毗奈耶中受持禁戒，而有闕漏；三者、有人即住於此受持禁戒，而不闕漏。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人住在外道惡說法及律中，外道也有外道法及律，此人受持外道的禁戒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種人是在佛善說法律中，受持佛所制定的戒律，可是沒有圓滿，有缺陷、有遺漏，不是完全持得非常清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人是安住佛善說法律中，受持佛所制定的戒律，持戒完全沒有缺失，沒有遺漏，是圓滿的境界。這是三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科配，以持戒的圓滿或缺失配釋下中上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4955"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初名下士，次名中士，後名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種持外道戒的人是下士；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種人受持佛法的戒律，但是沒有圓滿，是中士；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人受持佛法的禁戒，又完全圓滿沒有缺失遺漏，是上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、依受持戒心建立3　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科依受持戒心建立，約受戒時的動機分辨三士，分三科；第一科標，標示出三類人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於受持戒心建立三人。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又以受持淨戒的動機建立三類人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三種受戒心者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、有人為活命故，受持禁戒；二者、有人為生天故，受持禁戒；三者、有人為涅槃故，受持禁戒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人，為了活命而受持禁戒，在世間沒有辦法生存，而出家受戒，受戒後，接受供養能夠活下去；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種人，為了將來能夠生天（增上生）而受持禁戒；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人，為了追求涅槃（決定勝），發出離心以涅槃為上首而受持禁戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科配，以受戒的動機配釋下中上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初名下士，次名中士，後名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人，純粹為活命來受戒的是下士；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種人，為了生天來受戒的，是有所求的，是中士；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人，發出離心為了涅槃而持戒，是上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸四、依別解脫律儀建立3　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科依別解脫律儀建立，依別解脫律儀建立三士，分三科；第一科標，標出三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於受持別解脫律儀說有三人。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又受持別解脫律儀，就是具足戒，也可以建立三種人。律是佛說的禁制，儀就是行依律制，身口意依照禁制而行，稱為儀。律儀簡單說就是戒律，佛制的一條一條戒，若一條一條遵守，能得到各別各別的解脫，稱為別解脫律儀</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三種受持別解脫律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、有人唯能受持近住律儀；二者、有人亦能受持近事律儀；三者、有人亦能受持苾芻律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、有人只能受持近住律儀，一日一夜的八關齋戒，稱作近住律儀。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、有人也能受持近事律儀，就是優婆塞、優婆夷受的戒，主要是指五戒，廣說包括在家菩薩的四重二十八輕戒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、有人也能受比丘戒、比丘尼戒，這是第三種人。雖然只有說苾芻（比丘），也包括比丘尼。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4956"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科配，以受戒的種類配釋下中上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初名下士，次名中士，後名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人，只能受八關齋戒的人是下士，因為只有一日一夜，時間很短。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種人，能受八關齋戒，也能受持在家居士的五戒，這種人是中士，因為其盡形壽都要持這種戒。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人，能受八關齋戒、在家居士的五戒、也能受持具足戒，盡形壽受持，乃至受菩薩戒，盡未來際都持菩薩戒，這種人是上士。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　因為一個層次比一個層次更嚴格，要做到並不容易。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸五、依苾芻律儀建立3　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第五科依苾芻律儀建立，依受比丘戒辨別三士，分三科；第一科標，標出三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又於受持苾芻律儀說有三人。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又以出家受具足戒的人來說，也有三種人。此處是依比丘戒為例，比丘尼戒也包括在裡面。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三種受持苾芻律儀者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、有人唯能成就受具足支，無受隨法諸學處支，亦無隨護他人心支，亦無隨護如先所受諸學處支。二者、有人成前三支，無後一支。三者、有人具成四支。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人只能成就受具足支一種。出家以後去受具足戒，經過律師們一白三羯磨後，成為真正的比丘，「安住具戒」，稱作成就受具足支；但是沒有受「隨法諸學處支」，比丘應學的250條戒，名隨法諸學處支，雖然得到比丘戒體，可是沒有繼續學習受持別解脫戒，沒有「善能守護別解脫律儀」；也沒有受「隨護他人心支」，不能做到「軌則圓滿、所行圓滿」，不能夠受持譏嫌戒。不能做到軌則圓滿，是指於生活當中，行住坐臥等威儀路、搭衣持缽等所作事、或於正法受持讀誦乃至靜坐修止觀等善品加行處所，不能成就軌則，隨順世間，不越世間，隨順毗奈耶，不越毗奈耶；不能做到所行圓滿，是指不能做到不前往一、唱令家，二、婬女家，三、酤酒家，四、國王家，五、旃荼羅、羯恥那家等五種不應該去的處所。也沒有「隨護如先所受諸學處支」，是指不能「於犯微小罪見大怖畏、受學學處」，因此而不違犯；或是犯戒後能懺悔清淨。在日常持戒、修行及所作事當中，因為知道於微小罪生起大怖畏，能護持戒律不犯戒，或者是已經犯了，但是能夠慚愧，懂得懺悔，稱為「隨護」。做不到「隨護」，就是因為沒有「受學學處」。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種受戒的人是這樣，只做到「安住具戒」，不具足「善能守護別解脫律儀、軌則圓滿、所行圓滿、於犯微小罪見大怖畏、受學學處」。只是一個正式的比丘，其他對於戒條沒有去研究，沒有學習受持，對於日常生活當中行住坐臥，沒有做得很好，做錯了也不懂得懺悔，這是第一種人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種人，做到「安住具戒、善能守護別解脫律儀、軌則圓滿、所行圓滿」，不具足「於微小罪見大怖畏、受學學處」。「是正式的比丘，250條戒非常地明白，也能夠受持，在食衣住行這些事情都符合戒律，不該去的地方不去，入聚落的時候要注意哪些事情，也很清楚，但是做錯時不懂得懺悔，也不懂得千萬不要犯戒，沒有這種智慧知道業果的關係，因此沒有後一支。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人，做到「安住具戒、善能守護別解脫律儀、軌則圓滿、所行圓滿、於犯微小罪見大怖畏、受學學處」。四支（廣說包括六支）具足，是正式的比丘，對於250條戒很清楚，也充分的學習，又能受持，行住坐臥，不論出去、在寺裡都能夠護持譏嫌戒，各方面都做得很好，很謹慎護持所受的戒，也懂得護持他人的心，如果做錯時會即時懺悔，是一個名符其實的比丘。這是第三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科配，以持戒的種類配釋下中上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初名下士，次名中士，後名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人是下士，第二種人是中士，第三種人是上士，上士於受具足戒等四支（廣說包括六支）都能守護清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》唯能成就受具足支者：此中四支，如前已說應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/53.htm#49360:41037">陵本五十三卷六頁4226</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　此中所說的四支，在決擇〈五識身相應地意地〉卷53，1750頁裡面已經說過應當了知。〈五識身相應地意地〉卷53所說的四支，即卷22戒律儀所說六支。四支中第一支是「受具足支」，即「安住具戒」；第二支「受隨法學處支」，即「善能守護別解脫律儀」；第三支「隨護他心支」，即「軌則圓滿、所行圓滿」；第四支隨護如所受學處支，即「於犯微小罪見大怖畏、受學學處」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸六、依成就三種律儀建立3　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第六科依成就三種律儀建立，依成就別解脫戒、定共戒或道共戒分辨三士，分三科；第一科標，標出三類人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有三人。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又依成就三種戒說有三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4957"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出成就三種律儀者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、有人唯成別解脫律儀；二者、有人成別解脫、靜慮律儀；三者、有人成別解脫、靜慮、無漏三種律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、有的人只有成就別解脫戒，能夠受持比丘250條戒、比丘尼348條戒，外表清淨，但沒有修得禪定，內心不是那麼寂靜，還不完全清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、有的人除了成就別解脫戒以外，還時常修定降伏欲界的欲恚害尋思，證得禪定成就定共戒。定共戒有調伏內心煩惱的力量，有定的時候，欲界煩惱不現行，戒更清淨。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、有人成就別解脫戒、定共戒及道共戒。這只有聖人才能做到，其別解脫戒圓滿，也有禪定能調伏煩惱，還能夠成就聖道，斷除煩惱的種子，使令所持的戒真實究竟清淨。這是聖人的戒，聖人的戒最清淨，三種都具足。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科配，以持戒的種類與斷煩惱的差別配釋下中上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初名下士，次名中士，後名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種，只有成就別解脫律儀的人是下士；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種，成就別解脫戒與定共戒，具足這二種是中士；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種，三種律儀都具足的人，是上士，上品的持戒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸七、依成就一切所受律儀建立3　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第七科依成就一切所受律儀建立，約成就一切所受的律儀分辨三士，分三科；第一科標，標出三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有三人。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又依成就一切所受的律儀說有三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三種成就所受律儀者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、有人唯能成就非律儀非不律儀攝所受戒律儀；二者、有人亦能成就聲聞等相應所受戒律儀；三者、有人亦能成就菩提薩埵所受戒律儀。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、有人只能成就既不是佛教律儀之極善，也不是不律儀之極惡所受的戒律儀。能夠有世間的道德，世間道德也是一種戒。所持的世間戒律儀，不是極善，也不是極惡，能夠謹守身口意三業而行布施等，但力量不大。非律儀非不律儀是指既非佛教律儀之極善，也不是不律儀之極惡，而是隨緣應時而生起之善惡，即處中之善與處中之惡，這種善、惡之勢力很小，因此稱為處中之善惡。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、有人能夠成就聲聞乘相應的戒，包括在家居士的五戒，出家比丘戒、比丘尼戒等別解脫戒，直到盡形壽，死的時候就沒有了。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、有人能夠除了受別解脫戒還能受菩薩戒，菩薩戒是盡未來際都發願要持戒。不論在家、出家，如果能夠成就菩提薩埵所受的戒律儀，下一生再來，還會想起、憶起所受的菩薩戒，乃至經典裡面說，如果那時根本沒有佛法，也沒有戒師，自己自然就得到戒體。「薩埵」是有情，「菩提」是覺悟，菩提薩埵合起來稱為覺有情。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科配，以世間凡夫、聲聞、菩薩所受律儀的種類差別，配釋下中上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初名下士，次名中士，後名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種，世間的戒律儀是下士；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種，能夠成就聲聞別解脫戒是中士；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種，受菩薩戒，發願成佛的這種人是上士。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依所成就與所受的律儀來說，建立這三種人。這是約戒律來說，分七大科來說明三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬三、修所攝4　癸一、修習思惟方便建立3　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科修所攝，約修止觀分辨三士，分四科；第一科修習思惟方便建立，約內心修止觀時思惟的方法、過程來建立三士，分三科；第一科標，標出三人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4958"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復依修習思惟方便建立三人。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　&nbsp;又依止修習思惟止觀的過程方法，建立三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三種修習思惟方便者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、有人唯得勵力運轉思惟；二者、有人有間運轉，設得無間，要作功用方能運轉；三者、有人已得成就任運思惟。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　約於作意初修業者，初修欲界九心住時的狀況而言：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種人，只能勵力運轉思惟。修習止觀時要很努力才能使不斷向外攀緣的心安住在所緣境上，約九心住來說，這是內住、等住的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種人，成就有間斷運轉作意，修習止觀時雖然能夠安住在所緣境上，可是有時候又被色聲香味觸，貪瞋癡男女間斷，生起妄想，打斷所緣，使心沒有辦法完全安住在所緣境上，假設想得到沒有間斷的運轉作意，必須很努力才能夠成就。約九心住來說，安住、近住、調順、寂靜及最極寂靜時，內心還會有打閒岔的現象出現，還不是完全的沒有間斷得到止，屬於有間運轉作意；專注一趣屬於無間運轉作意，此時欲界定還沒有圓滿，對於所緣境還要有功用，要很努力才能夠專注一趣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種人，已經成就任運思惟。約九心住來說，這時心平等、心正直、心無功用住，成就等持的功德，此時若有輕安相應即成就未到地定，這時屬於任運思惟。這是約內心修止時的狀況建立三種人；修觀的道理從淺到深也是一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科配，以修止、修觀成就的差別配釋下中上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初名下士，次名中士，後名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種是下士；第二種是有間運轉，就算得到無間運轉，也必須有功用才能夠運轉，是中士；第三種人成就等持，欲界定已經圓滿又成就未到地定，這種人是上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#590000"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">《披》唯得勵力運轉思惟等者：此中差別，如本地分別釋應知。（<a href="http://mahabodhi.org/yoga/cb/11.htm#49382:9027">陵本十一卷十七頁922</a>）</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　唯得勵力運轉思惟等者，其中的差別，如〈本地分‧三摩呬多地〉卷11，385頁那裡有各別解釋，參考那裡所說就可以了解。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、依已得修差別建立3　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科依已得修差別建立，依已經得到止觀差別觀分辨三士，分三科；第一科標，先標出三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又依已得修差別故建立三人。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　依已經得到止、或者是得到觀這種人來建立三種人。已得修習禪定，成就修所成地。修是指內心要有定了，稱為修。如果散亂心修，都還不算是修行，因為沒有定力，專注力不夠，觀慧力量還不夠斷除煩惱，甚至調伏煩惱都沒有辦法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三種已得修者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、有人已得內心奢摩他定，未得增上慧法毗鉢舍那；二者、有人已得增上慧法毗鉢舍那，未得內心奢摩他定；三者、有人俱得二種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、有人已經成就內心根本奢摩他定，但是觀還不熟悉，毗鉢舍那還沒有成就。以「定」為依止修毗鉢舍那觀，能夠成就智慧，這種觀慧能幫助斷除煩惱，成就解脫，因此稱為增上慧。這種人是止強觀弱。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、有一種人的根性不同，適合修觀。觀慧已經成就，但是還沒有完全得到根本定，這是觀強止弱。這是以未到地定修四聖諦，未得根本定的初果聖人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、有一種人止觀兩種都成就了。若是成就出世道的止觀雙運，就是三果聖人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4959"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科配，以得到止或是得到觀的成就差別，配釋下中上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初名下士，次名中士，後名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種，是下士，只有止、沒有觀，調伏煩惱的力量如石壓草，但是還是不錯，是下士；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種，稱作中士，已經有觀，依止觀慧調伏煩惱的力量特別強。觀是智慧，止是定心，慧心所跟定心所不一樣，約智慧來說，第二種人的般若高一點，是中士；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種，止觀雙運以後，行者的定力夠、智慧也高，這種人是上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、依已得定地差別建立3　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科依已得定地差別建立，約已得定地差別建立三士，分三科；第一科標，標出三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又有三人。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又有三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三種已得定地差別者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、有人已得有尋有伺三摩地；二者、有人已得無尋唯伺三摩地；三者、有人已得無尋無伺三摩地。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、有人已經得到初禪有尋有伺三摩地。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、有人已經得到初禪與二禪中間的中間定即無尋唯伺定，成就大梵天王的定。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、有人已經得到二禪以上的無尋無伺定，這是第三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科配，以得到禪定的成就差別，配釋下中上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初名下士，次名中士，後名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種，成就初禪有尋有伺三摩地的人，是下士；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種，成就介於初禪和二禪中間定即無尋唯伺三摩地的人是中士；</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種，成就二禪以上無尋無伺三摩地的人是上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸四、依住修差別建立3　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科依住修差別建立，依住修差別建立三士，分三科；第一科標，標出三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">又依住修差別建立三人。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　又依止「住」，安住在內心禪修中的差別，建立三種人。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出三種住修差別者。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一者、有人住染汙靜慮；二者、有人住世間清淨靜慮；三者、有人住無漏靜慮。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、有人安住在染汙靜慮中，雖得到禪定，內心還有種種愛見慢疑無明的染汙心。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、有人安住在世間的清淨靜慮，能夠調伏愛見慢疑無明的煩惱，可是沒有根本斷除煩惱種子。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、有人安住在出世間的無漏靜慮，不但成就靜慮，更將愛見慢疑無明的煩惱種子也斷除，成就沒有煩惱流漏的靜慮，這是聖人的禪定。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4960"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、配</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科配，以禪定的有無染污，及煩惱種子有無斷除差別，配釋下中上士。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">初名下士，次名中士，後名上士。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第一種，成就染汙靜慮的人，外道也可能得到這種靜慮，這是下士。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種，成就世間清淨靜慮，是佛法的內道，離欲得到禪定，但是還沒有完全斷除煩惱種子的人，是中士。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三種，佛法中的聖人，已完全斷除煩惱種子，成就無漏靜慮，是上士。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是依十大科，建立下中上三士差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">庚二、十有情眾愛樂差別2　辛一、辨差別2　壬一、總標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科十有情眾愛樂差別，約十種有情所愛樂的對象不同建立三士，分二科；第一科辨差別，說明愛樂差別，又分二科；第一科總標，總相標出於十種法愛樂喜悅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，有十種有情眾，於十種法愛樂喜悅。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，有十種有情眾，對於十種法非常愛樂、非常喜悅。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、別列2　癸一、十法</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科別列，各別列出十種所愛樂法，分二科；第一科十法，十種法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等十法？一、壽，二、色，三、財，四、友，五、戒，六、聞，七、梵行，八、慧，九、法，十、生天。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　是哪十種法？一是壽命，歡喜長壽；二是姿色，喜歡容色光彩；三是財，金錢財物；四是友，歡喜朋友；五是戒，歡喜持戒；六是聞，歡喜聽聞佛法；七是梵行，歡喜修定，或是修無漏的聖道，這是屬於梵行；八是慧，歡喜世出世智慧，尤其是出世智慧；九是法，歡喜佛法；十是生天，歡喜將來能夠生天。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、十眾</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科十眾，十種有情眾生愛樂這十種法，雖然是這樣配，其實也不決定，是以多分來說是這樣。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">何等名為有情十眾？一、傍生，二、母邑，三、受用欲者，四、求所作者，五、出家者，六、多聞為命者，七、入證者，八、尋思者，九、勤苦者，十、棄身者。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　哪些稱為有情十眾？</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、畜生，畜生喜愛自己的壽命，畜生貪生怕死，人也是一樣，不過是相對來說。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、母邑，女人，女人喜歡外貌、容色美麗，所以女人喜歡色。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、受用欲，受用色聲香味觸五欲的人，需要很多金錢，因此愛樂、貪著財富。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、求所作者，想要有所作為，要作事業的人必須有朋友、同僚、屬下來幫助，因此愛樂喜悅朋友。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、出家者，愛樂持戒，出家基本上就是要持戒離欲。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、多聞為命者，有些人歡喜學習佛法，以聽聞佛法為生活重心，歡喜愛樂聽聞佛法，以此為基礎能成就、增長法身慧命。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、入證者，歡喜修止觀，喜歡梵行、離欲及斷除煩惱的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、尋思者，歡喜思惟觀察，一切法都要思惟觀察，喜歡智慧的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　九、勤苦者，這是精進的人，歡喜佛法，對於一切世出世間的善法都很歡喜，很精進學法，又能身體力行，依法而行的人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　十、棄身者，希望自己壽終以後可以生天，包括外道的邪梵行求，愛樂喜悅生天的法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以上是十種有情眾生，對於這十種法，有愛樂喜悅。這是配著說的，當然這裡面也有各式各樣的差別。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">辛二、隨料簡2　壬一、簡相違3　癸一、聞相違4　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨料簡，接著將重要的地方再思量簡別一番，分二科；第一科簡相違，簡別相違的情況，又分三科；第一科聞相違，聽聞佛法時，不應該作的事情，又分四科；第一科標，標出聞法者六種煩惱過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4961"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，聽聞正法者，略有六種煩惱過失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，聽聞佛法時，要略歸納起來有六種煩惱的過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出六種煩惱過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">謂憍慢過失、不欲過失、不信過失、身心損惱過失、散亂過失、迷惑過失。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　聽聞正法有六種煩惱過失。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、有憍傲、高慢的心，我慢高山法水不入，看不起說法師，法不能入心。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、不欲過失，只是聽聞，不想要深入學習佛法，不想依教奉行。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、不信過失，聽聞佛法了以後不相信，沒有生起信心。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、身心損惱過失，聽聞佛法了以後身體不舒服，心裡也不愉快，有種種的損惱，身麤重、心麤重。身心損惱過失也是聽聞正法中一種要避免的過失。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、散亂過失，聽聞佛法時不能很專注。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、迷惑過失，沒有分辨清楚，有疑，稱作迷惑過失。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　聽聞正法有疑，應當前往善知識處諮詢請問，有疑沒有問，心裡還是不能決定，聽了佛法以後不知道怎麼樣實踐，也是一種過失。接下來還會解釋。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子三、釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科釋，解釋。</span></span></span></div>
