<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">由如是等諸過失故，不能恭敬殷重聽法，廣說如經。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　有這些過失的時候，不能恭敬、誠懇、殷切尊重的聽法，如經典裡面有詳細說明這些過失。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子四、廣2　丑一、散亂</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科廣，再詳細說明煩惱過失，分二科；第一科散亂，散亂過失有二種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">散亂煩惱過失復有二種，謂說時散亂、說已散亂。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　聽聞佛法生出散亂過失又有二種：</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、說時散亂，是指法師說法時，內心不能專注，向外攀緣散亂。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、說已散亂，說完以後，聽者內心也不會繼續思惟所學習到的佛法，聽完以後不再複習，聽過就算了，沒有放在心裡，不當一回事，這時候是說已散亂。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　如何聽聞正法，請參考〈本地分‧菩薩地〉卷38，菩薩云何無雜染心及無散亂心聽聞正法共有十六相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丑二、迷惑</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科迷惑，迷惑過失是顛倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">迷惑者，謂顛倒。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　迷惑過失方面，是指顛倒。聞法者還不止是疑，更嚴重的是：當說法者說無常，聞法者聽成常；說苦，聽成樂，剛好聽錯了，稱作顛倒，這是迷惑過失。顛倒了，也會有疑惑，因此說迷惑，是指顛倒。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、梵行相違2　子一、略標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科梵行相違，與梵行相違的過失，分二科；第一科略標列，要略標示出三種煩惱發業。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，煩惱發業略有三種。一、相應發，二、親生發，三、增上發。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，煩惱發業，要略而言有三種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、相應發，造業剎那與煩惱同時發動，稱作相應發，造了業，障礙修習梵行。這是說造業的同時心有煩惱相應。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、親生發，煩惱引起發業，稱作親生發。煩惱是發業的近因，發起造作身口業。窺基大師說，身語意業一剎那與煩惱相應，稱作相應發。親生發，是指由煩惱發起身語意業。這是從因果說明，發業的因是煩惱，煩惱是因，發業是果。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、增上發，煩惱發起身語意業後，還繼續引發其他的煩惱，再發動其他的業。這是煩惱發業的延續力，用現代化說猶如蝴蝶效應，煩惱發業後能引發其他的煩惱，再發動其他的業，影響範圍很大。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、隨難釋</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科隨難釋，隨著解釋較困難的地方。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">引餘煩惱而發起故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　這是說明增上發，能引發其餘煩惱又發起諸業。例如本來只有瞋心，看到別的境界，又生起嫉妒心等，引發其他的煩惱又發起諸業，稱作增上發。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　以無明為例，第一種相應發是無明，無明與業同時生起，身語意業同時與無明在一起，稱作相應發。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二種親生發，親生發不是同時，是前一念的無明引生後一念的業，因為這樣想，接著就這樣作，稱作親生發。第一種情況是作的時候就有相應無明；第二種是先有煩惱，再發動行為，由煩惱而造業。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　增上發，是無明發出業以後，還引起其他的煩惱又發起諸業，本來是只有一種煩惱，無明相應發以後，造業時引生其他的貪瞋癡慢等煩惱，又再發起其他惡業。修梵行的人，是不應該有煩惱，也不應該再發業，要制伏煩惱，因此於此處安立煩惱發業為梵行相違。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4962"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、法相違2　子一、略標列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科法相違，法相違過失，分二科；第一科略標列，要略標示出六種非所愛法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，非所愛法略有六種。一、怨敵，二、疾病，三、不可愛境，四、生等諸苦，五、苦辛良藥，六、非串習善。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，眾生所不喜歡的法有六種。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、怨敵，怨敵聚會能生憂苦、治罰畏、惡名畏、傷害自己的生命、引發自己造惡墮三惡道等不可愛法，所以說怨家及敵人是非所愛法，所有眾生都不喜歡怨家及敵人。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、疾病，疾病能令身性變壞、憂苦增長多住、於可意境不喜受用、於不可意境非其所欲強受用、能令命根速離壞等不可愛法，沒有人喜歡生病，因此疾病也是眾所不喜歡的法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、不可愛境，色聲香味觸如果不可愛的、下劣的能令人生瞋，大家都不喜歡。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、生等諸苦，生老病死、愛別離、怨憎會苦等諸苦如前文所說，沒有一個眾生喜歡。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、苦辛良藥，又苦又辣的藥，能夠治病，以世間法來說，良藥苦口能治病。世間人又說良言苦口，話很難聽，可是真實語，可以改善自己的煩惱習氣，這也是苦辛良藥。以出世間來說，佛法可對治不良的習氣，以前習慣貪瞋癡，現在對治貪瞋癡，也是很苦，要吃佛法的藥也蠻苦的，完全依教奉行有時也會覺得很拘束，對有漏的凡夫來說，是一種苦辛良藥。佛法能夠治療煩惱病、心病，因此是良藥。良藥苦口，對有情而言是不可愛法。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、非串習善，止觀、戒定慧、聞思修，都不是眾生常常學習的善法，凡夫內心並不是常常安住正念裡面，稱為非串習善。非串習善不能引發可愛果，能令有情感得不可愛果。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、釋隨應</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科釋隨應，解釋應該要怎麼樣做。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">前四應遠離，後二應修習。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　前四種非可愛法應該要遠離，怨敵應該遠離；疾病也應該遠離，身體健康才能夠修行；不可愛境也應該遠離，以免生起瞋惱；生等諸苦也應該遠離。生，無知的凡夫還會喜歡，學了佛法就知道有生皆苦，老病死大家也不喜歡，因此生等諸苦也要遠離。後二是苦辛良藥的佛法與非串習善，應該要常常修習。若沒有修止觀，不能斷煩惱，應該常常聞思修，常常串習戒定慧這些善法。以上是「隨料簡」的第一科「簡相違」。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">壬二、辨受欲4　癸一、種類2　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科辨受欲，說明領受色聲香味觸欲的情況，分四科；第一科種類，受欲的種類，又分二科；第一科標，標出受欲有五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，受用諸欲略有五種。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，受用諸欲要略而言有五種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出五種受用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、領納受用，二、攝喜受用，三、尋思受用，四、貪彼受用，五、攝自受用。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、領納受用，領取納受境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、攝喜受用，攝取諸欲，歡喜受用。在受用欲境時，心情很愉快。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、尋思受用，經過觀察思惟以後，再受用欲的境界。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、貪彼受用，受用欲的時候，心裡有貪愛。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、攝自受用，凡夫總是攝受諸欲為自己所受用。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸二、過失2　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科過失，說明欲有種種的過失災患，分二科；第一科標，標出欲過八相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，諸欲過失略有八相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，諸欲的過失災患，要略歸納有八種相貌。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出欲的八種過失相。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4963"></a><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、少味多苦多過患相，二、他所逼切苦因緣相，三、雜染受用勝因緣相，四、墮諸惡趣苦因緣相，五、尋思擾亂苦因緣相，六、受用磨滅勝因緣相，七、喪身磨滅勝因緣相，八、能障善法勝因緣相。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、少味多苦多過患相，色聲香味觸五欲沒有什麼滋味，反而引生很多痛苦，所以說諸欲是少味多苦多過患相。例如食物吃下去，入口三寸即成糞，吃錯了，又會生病，有很多過患相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、他所逼切苦因緣相，為了得到欲，拼命去賺錢求得諸欲。求欲時，與他人之間，錢流來流去時，會有被逼切的痛苦；或是為了追逐男女之事，也會有彼此互相逼切苦，乃至衍生其他種種的苦，所以說諸欲是他所逼切苦的因緣相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、雜染受用勝因緣相，受用諸欲時，能於色聲香味觸引起貪心、瞋心、乃至愚癡心等煩惱雜染，因此諸欲是雜染受用的勝因緣相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、墮諸惡趣苦因緣相，因受用諸欲也會造種種的惡行，若造殺盜淫妄的業來取得諸欲，來生要到三惡道去受報，所以說諸欲是墮諸惡趣苦的因緣相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、尋思擾亂苦因緣相，受用諸欲時有種種尋思擾亂內心的苦，有了欲等尋思障礙，使自己不能得定生慧，所以說諸欲是尋思擾亂苦的因緣相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、受用磨滅勝因緣相，諸欲是無常的，受用諸欲也是無常的，無常來時，自身或諸欲變壞，就不能再受用殊勝的妙欲，所以說諸欲是受用磨滅的勝因緣相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　七、喪身磨滅勝因緣相，為了追逐諸欲，有可能造惡業，與他人結仇，導致喪失生命，或過度受用也會導致早夭，所以說諸欲是喪身磨滅的勝因緣相。例如俗話說人為財死，鳥為食亡，形容眾生為了食、為了財等諸欲，會喪身磨滅。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　八、能障善法勝因緣相，受用諸欲障礙修止及修觀。為了受用諸欲，忙著賺錢、忙著享受，也捨不得布施，不能潔身自愛、節儉受用，更沒有時間去聽聞、思惟佛法、修學止觀，因此說受用諸欲是能障善法的勝因緣相。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　多過患相是說欲能招感很多過患，苦因緣相是說欲是招苦的因緣，由此生出種種苦相；勝因緣相是說欲是導致某類法的最主要因緣，如文中說受用磨滅、喪身磨滅、能障善法等主要是由諸欲引發。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸三、變壞2　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科變壞，說明欲的變壞相，分二科；第一科標，標出六種。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，諸欲因緣略有六種變壞。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，各種欲的因緣，要略而言有六種變壞。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出六種變壞。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、他所逼切變壞，二、諸界互違變壞，三、所愛有情變壞，四、身變壞，五、心變壞，六、無常變壞。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、他所逼切變壞，諸欲為外力所逼迫而變壞，例如為欲而追求、積集、守護，會有地震、水火風災，及鬥爭偷盜搶騙等逼迫。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、諸界互違變壞，所受用的色聲香味觸是色法，是由地水火風所構成的，地水火風有變化，色聲香味觸也會有變壞。如同一個美女地大不調，可能就變胖、變壞，不再那麼美了。好的食物，若水分太多，容易發霉，也使令食物不再美好。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、所愛有情變壞，欲包括男女的欲，所愛的有情也會變壞，隨著時間、境界，身體生病，心情改變，移情別戀，種種的情況，使所愛的有情變壞。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、身變壞，身體變壞時，使令受用磨滅、或喪身磨滅，而不能受用諸欲。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、心變壞，受用欲時，使令心裡煩惱，稱作心變壞。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　六、無常變壞，由於無常、或是墮諸惡趣等種種的情況，而不能常常受用諸欲。總之欲是無常變化，不是一直那麼美好的，也不是一直能夠得到的。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">癸四、異名2　子一、標</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第四科異名，欲的另外一個名稱，分二科；第一科標，標出異名為稠林。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">復次，當知諸欲由五種相似法故，得稠林名。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　其次，應當知道諸欲由有五種相與世間稠密的樹林很像，因此諸欲另外一個名字稱作「稠林」。「稠林」是形容眾生內心的欲望和所受用的諸欲百味雜陳，像稠密樹林的花草樹木一樣，密密麻麻，不可計數。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">子二、列</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第二科列，列出五種相似法。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">一、由眾多相似法故；二、由雜穢相似法故；三、由養育眾生相似法故；四、由藏竄相似法故；五、由險難相似法故。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　一、由眾多相似法故，欲有很多種，如同稠林有很多花草樹木。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　二、由雜穢相似法故，受用欲時有很多種染污煩惱夾雜在一起，如同骯髒雜亂的稠林。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　三、由養育眾生相似法故，欲能夠養育各式各樣的眾生，在欲界裡的眾生都要有欲才能活下去，乃至禪定也是一種欲，是高級一點的欲。無色定也是一種欲，欲愛、有愛、無有愛，這些欲，三界眾生都還有，只是對象不同，層次不同，如同稠林能養育各種不同的動物。此處特別是指欲界諸欲。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　四、由藏竄相似法故，欲在三界眾生內心隱藏、跳動著，有欲在內心時，會有各式各樣的尋伺，使令心如小鹿般不斷地跳動，不斷地尋伺欲，如同諸多動物在稠林內隱藏、跳動一樣。</span></span></span></div>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　五、由險難相似法故，受用欲時，會有種種的危險，要跟他人競爭，有可能作惡業，墮到惡趣，乃至喪身磨滅，是險難相似法，如同稠林裡有各式各樣的毒蛇禽獸，到稠林去有很多危險災難。</span></span></span></div>

<p><a name="61p4964"></a><span style="font-size:medium"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">丁三、略不說餘</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　第三科略不說餘，〈有尋有伺等三地〉要略決擇至此，餘決擇文不再出現。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkblue"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">我已略說有尋有伺等三地決擇，其中處處餘決擇文，更不復現。</span></strong></span></span></p>

<div class="cb" style="margin-bottom:4px; margin-left:16px; margin-top:4px; text-align:start"><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:#002200"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">　我（彌勒菩薩）已經要略說明〈有尋有伺等三地〉的決擇。三界眾生各式各樣的情況，包括界施設建立，及三種雜染的煩惱雜染、業雜染及生雜染，已經作了要略的決斷簡擇，其他決斷簡擇的文章不會再重複出現了。彌勒菩薩只說到這裡為止。</span></span></span></div>

<p><span style="font-size:14pt"><span style="color:darkred"><strong><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;">瑜伽師地論科句披尋記卷第六十一</span></strong></span></span><br />
&nbsp;</p>
